theorem ind {x y: nat} (a: nat y) (px: wff x) (p0 pa py ps: wff y): $ x = a -> (px <-> pa) $ > $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ > $ x = y -> (px <-> py) $ > $ x = suc y -> (px <-> ps) $ > $ p0 $ > $ py -> ps $ > $ pa $;

theorem indd (G: wff) {x y: nat} (a: nat y) (px: wff x) (p0 pa py ps: wff y):
  $ x = a -> (px <-> pa) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = y -> (px <-> py) $ >
  $ x = suc y -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ G -> p0 $ >
  $ G /\ py -> ps $ >
  $ G -> pa $;

theorem indlt (G: wff) {x y: nat} (a: nat) (px: wff x) (p0 pa py ps: wff y):
  $ x = a -> (px <-> pa) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = y -> (px <-> py) $ >
  $ x = suc y -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ G -> p0 $ >
  $ G /\ y < a /\ py -> ps $ >
  $ G -> pa $;

local def gcd (a b: nat): nat;

theorem gcdeqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> gcd _a1 _b1 = gcd _a2 _b2 $;

theorem gcdeq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> gcd a _b1 = gcd a _b2 $;

theorem gcdcom (a b: nat): $ gcd a b = gcd b a $;

theorem gcd00: $ gcd 0 0 = 0 $;

theorem bgcd02 (a: nat): $ bgcd a 0 = a $;

theorem dvdbgcd (a b d: nat): $ d || a /\ d || b -> d || bgcd a b $;

theorem bgcddvd1lem (G: wff) (a b d q r u x y: nat):
  $ G -> a != 0 $ >
  $ G -> x * a = y * b + d $ >
  $ G -> b != 0 $ >
  $ G -> d * q + r = a $ >
  $ G -> x <= u $ >
  $ G -> y <= u $ >
  $ G -> suc ((u * b - x) * q) * a = (u * a - y) * q * b + r $;

theorem bgcddvd2lem (G: wff) (a b d q r u x y: nat):
  $ G -> a != 0 $ >
  $ G -> x * a = y * b + d $ >
  $ G -> b != 0 $ >
  $ G -> d * q + r = b $ >
  $ G -> x * q <= u $ >
  $ G -> y * q < u $ >
  $ G -> (u * b - x * q) * a = (u * a - suc (y * q)) * b + r $;

theorem bgcddvd1 (a b: nat): $ bgcd a b || a $;

theorem bgcddvd2 (a b: nat): $ a != 0 -> bgcd a b || b $;

abstract def rec (z: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): nat;

pub theorem recS (z: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): $ rec z S (suc n) = S @ rec z S n $;

theorem ocaseeq1 (_z1 _z2: nat) (S: set): $ _z1 = _z2 -> ocase _z1 S == ocase _z2 S $;

theorem ocaseeq2d (_G: wff) (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> ocase z _S1 == ocase z _S2 $;

theorem ocaseeq2 (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set): $ _S1 == _S2 -> ocase z _S1 == ocase z _S2 $;

theorem ocaseval (S: set) {i: nat} (n z: nat): $ ocase z S @ n = recn z (\ i, S @ fst i) n $;

theorem ocase0 (S: set) (z: nat): $ ocase z S @ 0 = z $;

theorem ocaseS (S: set) (n z: nat): $ ocase z S @ suc n = S @ n $;

local def ocasep (z: wff) (S: set): set;

theorem ocasepeqd (_G _z1 _z2: wff) (_S1 _S2: set): $ _G -> (_z1 <-> _z2) $ > $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> ocasep _z1 _S1 == ocasep _z2 _S2 $;

theorem ocasepeq (_z1 _z2: wff) (_S1 _S2: set): $ (_z1 <-> _z2) -> _S1 == _S2 -> ocasep _z1 _S1 == ocasep _z2 _S2 $;

theorem ocasepeq1d (_G _z1 _z2: wff) (S: set): $ _G -> (_z1 <-> _z2) $ > $ _G -> ocasep _z1 S == ocasep _z2 S $;

theorem ocasepeq1 (_z1 _z2: wff) (S: set): $ (_z1 <-> _z2) -> ocasep _z1 S == ocasep _z2 S $;

theorem ocasepeq2d (_G z: wff) (_S1 _S2: set): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> ocasep z _S1 == ocasep z _S2 $;

theorem ocasepeq2 (z: wff) (_S1 _S2: set): $ _S1 == _S2 -> ocasep z _S1 == ocasep z _S2 $;

theorem ocasep0 (S: set) (z: wff): $ 0 e. ocasep z S <-> z $;

theorem ocasepS (S: set) (n: nat) (z: wff): $ suc n e. ocasep z S <-> n e. S $;

abstract def obind (a: nat) (F: set): nat;

theorem obindeqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2: nat) (_F1 _F2: set): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> obind _a1 _F1 = obind _a2 _F2 $;

theorem obindeq (_a1 _a2: nat) (_F1 _F2: set): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _F1 == _F2 -> obind _a1 _F1 = obind _a2 _F2 $;

theorem obindeq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2: nat) (F: set): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> obind _a1 F = obind _a2 F $;

theorem obindeq1 (_a1 _a2: nat) (F: set): $ _a1 = _a2 -> obind _a1 F = obind _a2 F $;

theorem obindeq2d (_G: wff) (a: nat) (_F1 _F2: set): $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> obind a _F1 = obind a _F2 $;

theorem obindeq2 (a: nat) (_F1 _F2: set): $ _F1 == _F2 -> obind a _F1 = obind a _F2 $;

pub theorem obind0 (F: set): $ obind 0 F = 0 $;

pub theorem obindS (n: nat) (F: set): $ obind (suc n) F = F @ n $;

theorem obindS2 (n: nat) {x: nat}: $ obind n (\ x, suc x) = n $;

theorem obindeqS (F: set) (a: nat) {m: nat} (n: nat): $ obind n F = suc a <-> E. m (n = suc m /\ F @ m = suc a) $;

abstract def pow (a b: nat): nat;

theorem poweqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 ^ _b1 = _a2 ^ _b2 $;

theorem poweq (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> _a1 ^ _b1 = _a2 ^ _b2 $;

theorem poweq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 ^ b = _a2 ^ b $;

theorem poweq1 (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _a1 ^ b = _a2 ^ b $;

theorem poweq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> a ^ _b1 = a ^ _b2 $;

theorem poweq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> a ^ _b1 = a ^ _b2 $;

pub theorem pow0 (a: nat): $ a ^ 0 = 1 $;

pub theorem powS (a b: nat): $ a ^ suc b = a * a ^ b $;

theorem powS2 (a b: nat): $ a ^ suc b = a ^ b * a $;

theorem pow12 (a: nat): $ a ^ 1 = a $;

theorem pow22 (a: nat): $ a ^ 2 = a * a $;

theorem pow11 (b: nat): $ 1 ^ b = 1 $;

theorem powpos (a b: nat): $ 0 < a -> 0 < a ^ b $;

theorem powne0 (a b: nat): $ a != 0 -> a ^ b != 0 $;

theorem pow2ne0 (b: nat): $ 2 ^ b != 0 $;

theorem powltid2 (a b: nat): $ 1 < a -> b < a ^ b $;

theorem powadd (a b c: nat): $ a ^ (b + c) = a ^ b * a ^ c $;

theorem powmul (a b c: nat): $ a ^ (b * c) = (a ^ b) ^ c $;

theorem powdvd (a b c: nat): $ b <= c -> a ^ b || a ^ c $;

theorem powdvd1 (a b: nat): $ 0 < b -> a || a ^ b $;

theorem lepow2a (a b c: nat): $ a != 0 -> b <= c -> a ^ b <= a ^ c $;

theorem ltpow2 (a b c: nat): $ 1 < a -> (b < c <-> a ^ b < a ^ c) $;

theorem lepow2 (a b c: nat): $ 1 < a -> (b <= c <-> a ^ b <= a ^ c) $;

def shl (a n: nat): nat;

theorem shleqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> shl _a1 _n1 = shl _a2 _n2 $;

theorem shleq (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> shl _a1 _n1 = shl _a2 _n2 $;

theorem shleq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> shl _a1 n = shl _a2 n $;

theorem shleq1 (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> shl _a1 n = shl _a2 n $;

theorem shleq2d (_G: wff) (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> shl a _n1 = shl a _n2 $;

theorem shleq2 (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> shl a _n1 = shl a _n2 $;

def shr (a n: nat): nat;

theorem shreqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> shr _a1 _n1 = shr _a2 _n2 $;

theorem shreq (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> shr _a1 _n1 = shr _a2 _n2 $;

theorem shreq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> shr _a1 n = shr _a2 n $;

theorem shreq1 (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> shr _a1 n = shr _a2 n $;

theorem shreq2d (_G: wff) (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> shr a _n1 = shr a _n2 $;

theorem shreq2 (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> shr a _n1 = shr a _n2 $;

theorem shl01 (b: nat): $ shl 0 b = 0 $;

theorem shl02 (a: nat): $ shl a 0 = a $;

theorem shl11 (b: nat): $ shl 1 b = 2 ^ b $;

theorem shl12 (a: nat): $ shl a 1 = b0 a $;

theorem shlshl (a b c: nat): $ shl (shl a b) c = shl a (b + c) $;

theorem shladd (a b c: nat): $ shl (a + b) c = shl a c + shl b c $;

theorem shlpow2dvd (a b: nat): $ 2 ^ b || shl a b $;

theorem shl2dvd (a b: nat): $ 0 < b -> 2 || shl a b $;

theorem shr01 (b: nat): $ shr 0 b = 0 $;

theorem shr02 (a: nat): $ shr a 0 = a $;

theorem shr12 (a: nat): $ shr a 1 = a // 2 $;

theorem shrshr (a b c: nat): $ shr (shr a b) c = shr a (b + c) $;

theorem shrmodadd1 (a b c: nat): $ shr (a % 2 ^ (b + c)) b = shr a b % 2 ^ c $;

theorem shrmodadd2 (a b c: nat): $ shr (a % 2 ^ (b + c)) c = shr a c % 2 ^ b $;

theorem shrmodsub (a b c: nat): $ c <= b -> shr (a % 2 ^ b) c = shr a c % 2 ^ (b - c) $;

theorem shrshladdid (a b c: nat): $ c < 2 ^ b -> shr (shl a b + c) b = a $;

theorem shrshlid (a b: nat): $ shr (shl a b) b = a $;

theorem shrshl1 (a b c: nat): $ c <= b -> shr (shl a b) c = shl a (b - c) $;

theorem shrshl2 (a b c: nat): $ b <= c -> shr (shl a b) c = shr a (c - b) $;

theorem shreq0 (a b: nat): $ shr a b = 0 <-> a < 2 ^ b $;

def nel (a b: nat): wff;

theorem neleqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> (nel _a1 _b1 <-> nel _a2 _b2) $;

theorem neleq (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> (nel _a1 _b1 <-> nel _a2 _b2) $;

def ns (a: nat): set;

theorem nseqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> ns _a1 == ns _a2 $;

theorem nseq (_a1 _a2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> ns _a1 == ns _a2 $;

theorem elnel (a b: nat): $ a e. ns b <-> nel a b $;

theorem elneqd (G: wff) (a b c d: nat): $ G -> a = b $ > $ G -> c = d $ > $ G -> (a e. ns c <-> b e. ns d) $;

theorem elneq2d (G: wff) (a b c: nat): $ G -> b = c $ > $ G -> (a e. ns b <-> a e. ns c) $;

theorem elneq2 (a b c: nat): $ b = c -> (a e. ns b <-> a e. ns c) $;

theorem elneq (a b c d: nat): $ a = b -> c = d -> (a e. ns c <-> b e. ns d) $;

theorem appneq1d (G: wff) (f g x: nat): $ G -> f = g $ > $ G -> ns f @ x = ns g @ x $;

theorem appneq1 (f g x: nat): $ f = g -> ns f @ x = ns g @ x $;

theorem nfns {x: nat} (a: nat x): $ FN/ x a $ > $ FS/ x ns a $;

theorem el01 (a: nat): $ 0 e. ns a <-> odd a $;

theorem elshr (a b c: nat): $ a e. ns (shr b c) <-> a + c e. ns b $;

theorem elshl (a b c: nat): $ a e. ns (shl b c) <-> c <= a /\ a - c e. ns b $;

theorem elmodpow2 (a n x: nat): $ x e. ns (a % 2 ^ n) <-> x < n /\ x e. ns a $;

theorem shrss (a b n: nat): $ ns a C_ ns b -> ns (shr a n) C_ ns (shr b n) $;

theorem shlss (a b n: nat): $ ns a C_ ns b <-> ns (shl a n) C_ ns (shl b n) $;

theorem elb0 (a b: nat): $ a e. ns (b0 b) <-> 0 < a /\ a - 1 e. ns b $;

theorem elPower (A: set) (a: nat): $ a e. Power A <-> ns a C_ A $;

theorem powerfin (A: set): $ finite A -> finite (Power A) $;

def power (a: nat): nat;

theorem powereqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> power _a1 = power _a2 $;

theorem powereq (_a1 _a2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> power _a1 = power _a2 $;

theorem elpower (a b: nat): $ a e. ns (power b) <-> ns a C_ ns b $;

theorem powerupto (a: nat): $ power (upto a) = upto (2 ^ a) $;

def sUnion (A: set): set;

theorem unieqd (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> sUnion _A1 == sUnion _A2 $;

theorem unieq (_A1 _A2: set): $ _A1 == _A2 -> sUnion _A1 == sUnion _A2 $;

theorem elunii (A: set) (a b: nat): $ a e. A -> b e. ns a -> b e. sUnion A $;

theorem elssuni (A: set) (a: nat): $ a e. A -> ns a C_ sUnion A $;

theorem finuni (A: set): $ finite A -> finite (sUnion A) $;

theorem xabfin (A: set) (G: wff) {x: nat} (B: set x): $ G -> finite A $ > $ G /\ x e. A -> finite B $ > $ G -> finite (X\ x e. A, B) $;

theorem sabfin (A: set) (G: wff) {x y: nat} (B: set x): $ G -> y e. B -> x e. A $ > $ G -> finite A $ > $ G /\ x e. A -> finite B $ > $ G -> finite (S\ x, B) $;

def cons (a b: nat): nat;

theorem conseqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 : _b1 = _a2 : _b2 $;

theorem conseq (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> _a1 : _b1 = _a2 : _b2 $;

theorem conseq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 : b = _a2 : b $;

theorem conseq1 (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _a1 : b = _a2 : b $;

theorem conseq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> a : _b1 = a : _b2 $;

theorem conseq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> a : _b1 = a : _b2 $;

theorem consne0 (a b: nat): $ a : b != 0 $;

theorem ltconsid1 (a b: nat): $ a < a : b $;

theorem ltconsid2 (a b: nat): $ b < a : b $;

theorem consfstsnd (a: nat): $ a != 0 -> fst (a - 1) : snd (a - 1) = a $;

theorem excons (a: nat) {x y: nat}: $ a != 0 <-> E. x E. y a = x : y $;

theorem consinj (a b c d: nat): $ a : c = b : d <-> a = b /\ c = d $;

theorem conscan1 (a b c: nat): $ a : c = b : c <-> a = b $;

theorem conscan2 (a b c: nat): $ a : b = a : c <-> b = c $;

theorem consfst (a b: nat): $ fst (a : b - 1) = a $;

theorem conssnd (a b: nat): $ snd (a : b - 1) = b $;

theorem lecons1 (a b c: nat): $ a <= b <-> a : c <= b : c $;

theorem lecons2 (a b c: nat): $ b <= c <-> a : b <= a : c $;

theorem ltcons1 (a b c: nat): $ a < b <-> a : c < b : c $;

theorem ltcons2 (a b c: nat): $ b < c <-> a : b < a : c $;

abstract def sep (n: nat) (A: set): nat;

theorem sepeqd (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2: nat) (_A1 _A2: set): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> sep _n1 _A1 = sep _n2 _A2 $;

local def func (F A B: set): wff;

theorem funceqd (_G: wff) (_F1 _F2 _A1 _A2 _B1 _B2: set): $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> _B1 == _B2 $ > $ _G -> (func _F1 _A1 _B1 <-> func _F2 _A2 _B2) $;

theorem funceq (_F1 _F2 _A1 _A2 _B1 _B2: set): $ _F1 == _F2 -> _A1 == _A2 -> _B1 == _B2 -> (func _F1 _A1 _B1 <-> func _F2 _A2 _B2) $;

theorem funceq1d (_G: wff) (_F1 _F2 A B: set): $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> (func _F1 A B <-> func _F2 A B) $;

theorem funceq1 (_F1 _F2 A B: set): $ _F1 == _F2 -> (func _F1 A B <-> func _F2 A B) $;

theorem funceq2d (_G: wff) (F _A1 _A2 B: set): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> (func F _A1 B <-> func F _A2 B) $;

theorem funceq2 (F _A1 _A2 B: set): $ _A1 == _A2 -> (func F _A1 B <-> func F _A2 B) $;

theorem funceq3d (_G: wff) (F A _B1 _B2: set): $ _G -> _B1 == _B2 $ > $ _G -> (func F A _B1 <-> func F A _B2) $;

theorem funceq3 (F A _B1 _B2: set): $ _B1 == _B2 -> (func F A _B1 <-> func F A _B2) $;

theorem nffunc {x: nat} (F A B: set x): $ FS/ x F $ > $ FS/ x A $ > $ FS/ x B $ > $ F/ x func F A B $;

theorem funcisf (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> isfun F $;

theorem funcdm (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> Dom F == A $;

theorem funcrn (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> Ran F C_ B $;

theorem funcss3 (A B C F: set): $ B C_ C -> func F A B -> func F A C $;

theorem funcal (A B F: set) {x: nat}: $ func F A B <-> isfun F /\ Dom F == A /\ A. x (x e. A -> F @ x e. B) $;

theorem funcres (A B C F: set): $ func F A B /\ C C_ A -> func (F |` C) C B $;

theorem funcssxp (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> F C_ Xp A B $;

theorem funcfin (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> finite A -> finite B -> finite F $;

theorem funcT (A B F: set) (x: nat): $ func F A B /\ x e. A -> F @ x e. B $;

theorem eqfunc (A B C F G: set) {x: nat}: $ func F A B /\ func G A C -> (F == G <-> A. x (x e. A -> F @ x = G @ x)) $;

theorem funceq0 (A B F: set): $ func F A B -> (F == ns 0 <-> A == ns 0) $;

theorem func02 (B F: set): $ func F (ns 0) B <-> F == ns 0 $;

theorem func03 (A F: set): $ func F A (ns 0) <-> F == ns 0 /\ A == ns 0 $;

theorem unfunc (A1 A2 B F1 F2: set) (G: wff): $ G -> A1 i^i A2 == ns 0 $ > $ G -> func F1 A1 B $ > $ G -> func F2 A2 B $ > $ G -> func (F1 u. F2) (A1 u. A2) B $;

theorem funcappb (A B F: set) (a b: nat): $ func F A B -> (a <> b e. F <-> a e. A /\ F @ a = b) $;

def Arrow (A B: set): set;

theorem Arroweqd (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2 _B1 _B2: set): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> _B1 == _B2 $ > $ _G -> Arrow _A1 _B1 == Arrow _A2 _B2 $;

theorem Arroweq (_A1 _A2 _B1 _B2: set): $ _A1 == _A2 -> _B1 == _B2 -> Arrow _A1 _B1 == Arrow _A2 _B2 $;

theorem Arroweq1d (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2 B: set): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> Arrow _A1 B == Arrow _A2 B $;

theorem Arroweq1 (_A1 _A2 B: set): $ _A1 == _A2 -> Arrow _A1 B == Arrow _A2 B $;

theorem Arroweq2d (_G: wff) (A _B1 _B2: set): $ _G -> _B1 == _B2 $ > $ _G -> Arrow A _B1 == Arrow A _B2 $;

theorem Arroweq2 (A _B1 _B2: set): $ _B1 == _B2 -> Arrow A _B1 == Arrow A _B2 $;

theorem Arrowisf (A B: set) (f: nat): $ f e. Arrow A B -> isfun (ns f) $;

theorem Arrowdm (A B: set) (f: nat): $ f e. Arrow A B -> Dom (ns f) == A $;

theorem Arrowfin (A B: set): $ finite A -> finite B -> finite (Arrow A B) $;

theorem appT (A B: set) (f x: nat): $ f e. Arrow A B /\ x e. A -> ns f @ x e. B $;

theorem Arrow01 (B: set): $ Arrow (ns 0) B == ns (sn 0) $;

theorem Arrow02 (A: set): $ ~A == ns 0 -> Arrow A (ns 0) == ns 0 $;

def rlam {x: nat} (a: nat) (v: nat x): nat;

theorem rlameqd (_G: wff) {x: nat} (_a1 _a2 _v1 _v2: nat x): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> \. x e. _a1, _v1 = \. x e. _a2, _v2 $;

theorem rlameq2d (_G: wff) {x: nat} (a _v1 _v2: nat x): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> \. x e. a, _v1 = \. x e. a, _v2 $;

theorem rlameqs {x: nat} (a b: nat x): $ ns (\. x e. a, b) == (\ x, b) |` ns a $;

theorem elrlam (p: nat) {x: nat} (a: nat) (b: nat x): $ p e. ns (\. x e. a, b) <-> E. x (x e. ns a /\ p = x <> b) $;

theorem nfrlam {x y: nat} (a b: nat x y): $ FN/ x a $ > $ FN/ x b $ > $ FN/ x \. y e. a, b $;

theorem unrlam (a b c: nat) {x: nat} (v: nat x): $ ns (\. x e. a, v) u. ns (\. x e. b, v) == ns (\. x e. c, v) <-> ns a u. ns b == ns c $;

theorem apprlams (a: nat) {x: nat} (b c: nat x): $ c e. ns a -> ns (\. x e. a, b) @ c = N[c / x] b $;

theorem apprlamed (G: wff) (a c d: nat) {x: nat} (b: nat x): $ G /\ x = c -> b = d $ > $ G -> c e. ns a $ > $ G -> ns (\. x e. a, b) @ c = d $;

theorem apprlamed1 (G P: wff) (a c f: nat) {x: nat} (b: nat x): $ G -> c e. ns a $ > $ G /\ x = c -> ns f @ c = b -> P $ > $ G -> f = \. x e. a, b -> P $;

theorem eqrlam (a f: nat) {x: nat} (b: nat x): $ f = \. x e. a, b <-> isfun (ns f) /\ Dom (ns f) == ns a /\ A. x (x e. ns a -> ns f @ x = b) $;

def write (F: set) (a b: nat): set;

theorem writeeqd (_G: wff) (_F1 _F2: set) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> write _F1 _a1 _b1 == write _F2 _a2 _b2 $;

theorem writeeq (_F1 _F2: set) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _F1 == _F2 -> _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> write _F1 _a1 _b1 == write _F2 _a2 _b2 $;

theorem writeeq1d (_G: wff) (_F1 _F2: set) (a b: nat): $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ > $ _G -> write _F1 a b == write _F2 a b $;

theorem writeeq1 (_F1 _F2: set) (a b: nat): $ _F1 == _F2 -> write _F1 a b == write _F2 a b $;

theorem writeeq2d (_G: wff) (F: set) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> write F _a1 b == write F _a2 b $;

theorem writeeq2 (F: set) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> write F _a1 b == write F _a2 b $;

theorem writeeq3d (_G: wff) (F: set) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> write F a _b1 == write F a _b2 $;

theorem writeeq3 (F: set) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> write F a _b1 == write F a _b2 $;

theorem elwrite (F: set) (a b x y: nat): $ x <> y e. write F a b <-> ifp (x = a) (y = b) (x <> y e. F) $;

pub theorem writeEq (F: set) (a b: nat): $ write F a b @ a = b $;

pub theorem writeNe (F: set) (a b x: nat): $ x != a -> write F a b @ x = F @ x $;

theorem writeisf (F: set) (a b: nat): $ isfun F -> isfun (write F a b) $;

theorem writeres (F: set) (a b: nat) {x: nat}: $ write F a b == (F |` {x | x != a}) u. ns (sn (a <> b)) $;

theorem writefin (F: set) (a b: nat): $ finite F -> finite (write F a b) $;

theorem dmwrite (F: set) (a b: nat): $ Dom (write F a b) == Dom F u. ns (sn a) $;

theorem rnwrite (F: set) (a b: nat): $ Ran (write F a b) C_ Ran F u. ns (sn b) $;

theorem writeArrow (A B: set) (G: wff) (a b f g: nat): $ G -> f e. Arrow A B $ > $ G -> a e. A $ > $ G -> b e. B $ > $ G -> write (ns f) a b == ns g $ > $ G -> g e. Arrow A B $;

local def srecaux (S: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem srecauxeqd (_G: wff) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srecaux _S1 _n1 = srecaux _S2 _n2 $;

theorem srecauxeq (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> srecaux _S1 _n1 = srecaux _S2 _n2 $;

theorem srecauxeq1d (_G: wff) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> srecaux _S1 n = srecaux _S2 n $;

theorem srecauxeq1 (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> srecaux _S1 n = srecaux _S2 n $;

theorem srecauxeq2d (_G: wff) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srecaux S _n1 = srecaux S _n2 $;

theorem srecauxeq2 (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> srecaux S _n1 = srecaux S _n2 $;

theorem srecaux0 (S: set): $ srecaux S 0 = 0 $;

theorem srecauxS (S: set) (n: nat): $ ns (srecaux S (suc n)) == write (ns (srecaux S n)) n (S @ srecaux S n) $;

theorem dmsrecaux (S: set) (n: nat): $ Dom (ns (srecaux S n)) == ns (upto n) $;

theorem srecauxisf (S: set) (n: nat): $ isfun (ns (srecaux S n)) $;

abstract def srec (S: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem sreceqd (_G: wff) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srec _S1 _n1 = srec _S2 _n2 $;

theorem sreceq (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> srec _S1 _n1 = srec _S2 _n2 $;

theorem sreceq1d (_G: wff) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> srec _S1 n = srec _S2 n $;

theorem sreceq1 (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> srec _S1 n = srec _S2 n $;

theorem sreceq2d (_G: wff) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srec S _n1 = srec S _n2 $;

theorem sreceq2 (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> srec S _n1 = srec S _n2 $;

theorem srecauxapp (S: set) (a n: nat): $ a < n -> ns (srecaux S n) @ a = srec S a $;

theorem srecval2 (S: set) (n: nat): $ srec S n = S @ srecaux S n $;

theorem srecres (S: set) {i: nat} (n: nat): $ (\ i, srec S i) |` ns (upto n) == ns (srecaux S n) $;

theorem srecrlam (S: set) {i: nat} (n: nat): $ \. i e. upto n, srec S i = srecaux S n $;

theorem sreclem (f n: nat) {x: nat} (a: nat x): $ f = \. x e. upto n, a -> size (Dom (ns f)) = n $;

theorem sreclem2 (f n: nat) {x: nat} (a b: nat x): $ f = \. x e. upto n, a -> b < n -> ns f @ b = N[b / x] a $;

pub theorem srecval {i: nat} (S: set) (n: nat): $ srec S n = S @ (\. i e. upto n, srec S i) $;

local def srecpaux (A: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem srecpauxeqd (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srecpaux _A1 _n1 = srecpaux _A2 _n2 $;

theorem srecpauxeq (_A1 _A2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> srecpaux _A1 _n1 = srecpaux _A2 _n2 $;

theorem srecpauxeq1d (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> srecpaux _A1 n = srecpaux _A2 n $;

theorem srecpauxeq1 (_A1 _A2: set) (n: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> srecpaux _A1 n = srecpaux _A2 n $;

theorem srecpauxeq2d (_G: wff) (A: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> srecpaux A _n1 = srecpaux A _n2 $;

theorem srecpauxeq2 (A: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> srecpaux A _n1 = srecpaux A _n2 $;

abstract def srecp (A: set) (n: nat): wff;

theorem srecpeqd (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (srecp _A1 _n1 <-> srecp _A2 _n2) $;

theorem srecpeq (_A1 _A2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> (srecp _A1 _n1 <-> srecp _A2 _n2) $;

theorem srecpeq1d (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> (srecp _A1 n <-> srecp _A2 n) $;

theorem srecpeq1 (_A1 _A2: set) (n: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> (srecp _A1 n <-> srecp _A2 n) $;

theorem srecpeq2d (_G: wff) (A: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (srecp A _n1 <-> srecp A _n2) $;

theorem srecpeq2 (A: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> (srecp A _n1 <-> srecp A _n2) $;

theorem srecpauxval (A: set) {i: nat} (n: nat): $ srecpaux A n = nat (n <> sep (upto n) {i | srecp A i} e. A) $;

pub theorem srecpval {i: nat} (A: set) (n: nat): $ srecp A n <-> n <> sep (upto n) {i | srecp A i} e. A $;

abstract def card (s: nat): nat;

theorem cardeqd (_G: wff) (_s1 _s2: nat): $ _G -> _s1 = _s2 $ > $ _G -> card _s1 = card _s2 $;

theorem cardeq (_s1 _s2: nat): $ _s1 = _s2 -> card _s1 = card _s2 $;

theorem cardvallem {i: nat} (n: nat): $ card n = ((\ i, card i) |` ns (upto n)) @ (n // 2) + n % 2 $;

pub theorem card0: $ card 0 = 0 $;

theorem cardval (n: nat): $ n != 0 -> card n = card (n // 2) + n % 2 $;

theorem cardb0 (n: nat): $ card (b0 n) = card n $;

theorem cardb1 (n: nat): $ card (b1 n) = suc (card n) $;

pub theorem cardS (a s: nat): $ ~a e. ns s -> card (a ; s) = suc (card s) $;

abstract def lrec (z: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem lreceqd (_G: wff) (_z1 _z2: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ > $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> lrec _z1 _S1 _n1 = lrec _z2 _S2 _n2 $;

theorem lreceq (_z1 _z2: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _z1 = _z2 -> _S1 == _S2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> lrec _z1 _S1 _n1 = lrec _z2 _S2 _n2 $;

theorem lreceq1d (_G: wff) (_z1 _z2: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ > $ _G -> lrec _z1 S n = lrec _z2 S n $;

theorem lreceq1 (_z1 _z2: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): $ _z1 = _z2 -> lrec _z1 S n = lrec _z2 S n $;

theorem lreceq2d (_G: wff) (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> lrec z _S1 n = lrec z _S2 n $;

theorem lreceq2 (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> lrec z _S1 n = lrec z _S2 n $;

theorem lreceq3d (_G: wff) (z: nat) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> lrec z S _n1 = lrec z S _n2 $;

theorem lreceq3 (z: nat) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> lrec z S _n1 = lrec z S _n2 $;

theorem lrecval (S: set) (n z: nat): $ lrec z S n = if (n = 0) z (S @ (fst (n - 1) <> snd (n - 1) <> lrec z S (snd (n - 1)))) $;

pub theorem lrec0 (z: nat) (S: set): $ lrec z S 0 = z $;

pub theorem lrecS (z: nat) (S: set) (a b: nat): $ lrec z S (a : b) = S @ (a <> b <> lrec z S b) $;

theorem listindd (G: wff) {x a l: nat} (n: nat) (px: wff x) (p0 pn: wff) (pl: wff l) (ps: wff a l):
  $ x = n -> (px <-> pn) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = l -> (px <-> pl) $ >
  $ x = a : l -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ G -> p0 $ >
  $ G /\ pl -> ps $ >
  $ G -> pn $;

theorem listind {x a l: nat} (n: nat) (px: wff x) (p0 pn: wff) (pl: wff l) (ps: wff a l):
  $ x = n -> (px <-> pn) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = l -> (px <-> pl) $ >
  $ x = a : l -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ p0 $ >
  $ pl -> ps $ >
  $ pn $;

theorem lmemeqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _l1 _l2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (_a1 IN _l1 <-> _a2 IN _l2) $;

theorem lmemeq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 l: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> (_a1 IN l <-> _a2 IN l) $;

theorem lmemeq1 (_a1 _a2 l: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> (_a1 IN l <-> _a2 IN l) $;

theorem lmemeq2d (_G: wff) (a _l1 _l2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (a IN _l1 <-> a IN _l2) $;

theorem lmemeq2 (a _l1 _l2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> (a IN _l1 <-> a IN _l2) $;

theorem lmem0 (a: nat): $ ~a IN 0 $;

theorem lmem1 (a b: nat): $ a IN b : 0 <-> a = b $;

def all (A: set) (l: nat): wff;

theorem alleqd (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (_l1 _l2: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (all _A1 _l1 <-> all _A2 _l2) $;

theorem alleq (_A1 _A2: set) (_l1 _l2: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> _l1 = _l2 -> (all _A1 _l1 <-> all _A2 _l2) $;

theorem alleq1d (_G: wff) (_A1 _A2: set) (l: nat): $ _G -> _A1 == _A2 $ > $ _G -> (all _A1 l <-> all _A2 l) $;

theorem alleq1 (_A1 _A2: set) (l: nat): $ _A1 == _A2 -> (all _A1 l <-> all _A2 l) $;

theorem alleq2d (_G: wff) (A: set) (_l1 _l2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (all A _l1 <-> all A _l2) $;

theorem alleq2 (A: set) (_l1 _l2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> (all A _l1 <-> all A _l2) $;

theorem all0 (A: set): $ all A 0 $;

theorem allS (A: set) (a b: nat): $ all A (a : b) <-> a e. A /\ all A b $;

theorem all1 (A: set) (a: nat): $ all A (a : 0) <-> a e. A $;

theorem allal2 (A: set) (l: nat) {x: nat}: $ all A l <-> A. x (x IN l -> x e. A) $;

theorem allal (l: nat) {x: nat} (p: wff x): $ all {x | p} l <-> A. x (x IN l -> p) $;

theorem elall (A: set) (l x: nat): $ all A l -> x IN l -> x e. A $;

theorem ssall (A B: set) (l: nat): $ A C_ B -> all A l -> all B l $;

abstract def nth (n l: nat): nat;

abstract def repeat (a n: nat): nat;

theorem repeateqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> repeat _a1 _n1 = repeat _a2 _n2 $;

theorem repeateq (_a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> repeat _a1 _n1 = repeat _a2 _n2 $;

theorem repeateq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> repeat _a1 n = repeat _a2 n $;

theorem repeateq1 (_a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> repeat _a1 n = repeat _a2 n $;

theorem repeateq2d (_G: wff) (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> repeat a _n1 = repeat a _n2 $;

theorem repeateq2 (a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> repeat a _n1 = repeat a _n2 $;

pub theorem repeat0 (a: nat): $ repeat a 0 = 0 $;

pub theorem repeatS (a n: nat): $ repeat a (suc n) = a : repeat a n $;

theorem repeat1 (a: nat): $ repeat a 1 = a : 0 $;

theorem repeatlen (a n: nat): $ len (repeat a n) = n $;

theorem repeatadd (a m n: nat): $ repeat a (m + n) = repeat a m ++ repeat a n $;

theorem repeatT (A: set) (a n: nat): $ a e. A -> repeat a n e. List A $;

theorem repeatArray (A: set) (a n: nat): $ a e. A -> repeat a n e. Array A n $;

local def grecaux1 (K: set) (x z n: nat): nat;

theorem grecaux1eqd (_G: wff) (_K1 _K2: set) (_x1 _x2 _z1 _z2 _n1 _n2: nat):
  $ _G -> _K1 == _K2 $ >
  $ _G -> _x1 = _x2 $ >
  $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ >
  $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ >
  $ _G -> grecaux1 _K1 _x1 _z1 _n1 = grecaux1 _K2 _x2 _z2 _n2 $;

theorem grecaux1eq (_K1 _K2: set) (_x1 _x2 _z1 _z2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _K1 == _K2 -> _x1 = _x2 -> _z1 = _z2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> grecaux1 _K1 _x1 _z1 _n1 = grecaux1 _K2 _x2 _z2 _n2 $;

theorem grecaux1eq1d (_G: wff) (_K1 _K2: set) (x z n: nat): $ _G -> _K1 == _K2 $ > $ _G -> grecaux1 _K1 x z n = grecaux1 _K2 x z n $;

theorem grecaux1eq1 (_K1 _K2: set) (x z n: nat): $ _K1 == _K2 -> grecaux1 _K1 x z n = grecaux1 _K2 x z n $;

theorem grecaux1eq2d (_G: wff) (K: set) (_x1 _x2 z n: nat): $ _G -> _x1 = _x2 $ > $ _G -> grecaux1 K _x1 z n = grecaux1 K _x2 z n $;

theorem grecaux1eq2 (K: set) (_x1 _x2 z n: nat): $ _x1 = _x2 -> grecaux1 K _x1 z n = grecaux1 K _x2 z n $;

local def grecaux2 (z: nat) (K F: set) (x n k: nat): nat;

  $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ >
  $ _G -> _K1 == _K2 $ >
  $ _G -> _F1 == _F2 $ >
  $ _G -> _x1 = _x2 $ >
  $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> grecaux2 _z1 _K1 _F1 _x1 _n1 _k1 = grecaux2 _z2 _K2 _F2 _x2 _n2 _k2 $;

local def rev (l: nat): nat;

theorem revsn (a: nat): $ rev (a : 0) = a : 0 $;

theorem revappend (l1 l2: nat): $ rev (l1 ++ l2) = rev l2 ++ rev l1 $;

theorem revsnoc (a l: nat): $ rev (l |> a) = a : rev l $;

theorem revrev (l: nat): $ rev (rev l) = l $;

theorem revinj (l l2: nat): $ rev l = rev l2 <-> l = l2 $;

theorem reveq0 (l: nat): $ rev l = 0 <-> l = 0 $;

theorem exsnoc {a: nat} (l: nat) {l2: nat}: $ l != 0 <-> E. l2 E. a l = l2 |> a $;

theorem snocinj (a b l1 l2: nat): $ l1 |> a = l2 |> b <-> l1 = l2 /\ a = b $;

theorem appendcan2 (a b c: nat): $ a ++ c = b ++ c <-> a = b $;

local def lfn (F: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem nthext (l1 l2: nat) {n: nat}: $ l1 = l2 <-> A. n nth n l1 = nth n l2 $;

local def drop (l n: nat): nat;

theorem dropeqd (_G: wff) (_l1 _l2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> drop _l1 _n1 = drop _l2 _n2 $;

theorem dropeq (_l1 _l2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> drop _l1 _n1 = drop _l2 _n2 $;

theorem dropeq1d (_G: wff) (_l1 _l2 n: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> drop _l1 n = drop _l2 n $;

theorem dropeq1 (_l1 _l2 n: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> drop _l1 n = drop _l2 n $;

theorem dropeq2d (_G: wff) (l _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> drop l _n1 = drop l _n2 $;

theorem dropeq2 (l _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> drop l _n1 = drop l _n2 $;

theorem takelen (l n: nat): $ len (take l n) = min (len l) n $;

theorem droplen (l n: nat): $ len (drop l n) = len l - n $;

theorem takenth (i l n: nat): $ i < n -> nth i (take l n) = nth i l $;

theorem takenth0 (i l n: nat): $ n <= i -> nth i (take l n) = 0 $;

theorem dropnth (i l n: nat): $ nth i (drop l n) = nth (i + n) l $;

theorem takedrop (l n: nat): $ take l n ++ drop l n = l $;

theorem take0 (l: nat): $ take l 0 = 0 $;

theorem drop0 (l: nat): $ drop l 0 = l $;

theorem dropall (l n: nat): $ len l <= n -> drop l n = 0 $;

theorem takeall (l n: nat): $ len l <= n -> take l n = l $;

theorem takemin (l n: nat): $ take l (min (len l) n) = take l n $;

theorem takeappend1 (l1 l2 n: nat): $ n <= len l1 -> take (l1 ++ l2) n = take l1 n $;

theorem appendinj1 (l1 l2 r1 r2: nat): $ len l1 = len r1 -> (l1 ++ l2 = r1 ++ r2 <-> l1 = r1 /\ l2 = r2) $;

theorem appendinj2 (l1 l2 r1 r2: nat): $ len l2 = len r2 -> (l1 ++ l2 = r1 ++ r2 <-> l1 = r1 /\ l2 = r2) $;

def sublistAt (n L1 L2: nat): wff;

theorem sublistAteqd (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2 _L11 _L12 _L21 _L22: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> _L11 = _L12 $ > $ _G -> _L21 = _L22 $ > $ _G -> (sublistAt _n1 _L11 _L21 <-> sublistAt _n2 _L12 _L22) $;

theorem sublistAteq (_n1 _n2 _L11 _L12 _L21 _L22: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> _L11 = _L12 -> _L21 = _L22 -> (sublistAt _n1 _L11 _L21 <-> sublistAt _n2 _L12 _L22) $;

theorem sublistAteq1d (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2 L1 L2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (sublistAt _n1 L1 L2 <-> sublistAt _n2 L1 L2) $;

theorem sublistAteq1 (_n1 _n2 L1 L2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> (sublistAt _n1 L1 L2 <-> sublistAt _n2 L1 L2) $;

theorem sublistAteq2d (_G: wff) (n _L11 _L12 L2: nat): $ _G -> _L11 = _L12 $ > $ _G -> (sublistAt n _L11 L2 <-> sublistAt n _L12 L2) $;

theorem sublistAteq2 (n _L11 _L12 L2: nat): $ _L11 = _L12 -> (sublistAt n _L11 L2 <-> sublistAt n _L12 L2) $;

theorem sublistAteq3d (_G: wff) (n L1 _L21 _L22: nat): $ _G -> _L21 = _L22 $ > $ _G -> (sublistAt n L1 _L21 <-> sublistAt n L1 _L22) $;

theorem sublistAteq3 (n L1 _L21 _L22: nat): $ _L21 = _L22 -> (sublistAt n L1 _L21 <-> sublistAt n L1 _L22) $;

theorem sublistAtT (A: set) (L1 L2 n: nat): $ sublistAt n L1 L2 -> L1 e. List A -> L2 e. List A $;

theorem sublistAt_append (l l1 l2 n: nat): $ sublistAt n l (l1 ++ l2) <-> sublistAt n l l1 /\ sublistAt (n + len l1) l l2 $;

theorem sublistAt_len_le (L1 L2 n: nat): $ sublistAt n L1 L2 -> n + len L2 <= len L1 $;

theorem sublistAt_left (L1 L2 l n: nat): $ sublistAt n L1 L2 -> sublistAt n (L1 ++ l) L2 $;

theorem sublistAt_right (L1 L2 l n: nat): $ sublistAt n L1 L2 -> sublistAt (len l + n) (l ++ L1) L2 $;

theorem sublistAt_id (L: nat): $ sublistAt 0 L L $;

def all2 (R: set): set;

theorem all2eqd (_G: wff) (_R1 _R2: set): $ _G -> _R1 == _R2 $ > $ _G -> all2 _R1 == all2 _R2 $;

theorem all2eq (_R1 _R2: set): $ _R1 == _R2 -> all2 _R1 == all2 _R2 $;

theorem elall2 (R: set) (l1 l2: nat) {n x y: nat}: $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 R <-> len l1 = len l2 /\ A. n A. x A. y (nth n l1 = suc x -> nth n l2 = suc y -> x <> y e. R) $;

theorem elall22 (R: set) (l1 l2: nat) {n x y: nat}: $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 R <-> len l1 = len l2 /\ A. n A. x (nth n l1 = suc x -> A. y (nth n l2 = suc y -> x <> y e. R)) $;

theorem all2ssg (R S: set) (l1 l2: nat) {x y: nat}: $ A. x A. y (x IN l1 /\ y IN l2 -> x <> y e. R -> x <> y e. S) -> l1 <> l2 e. all2 R -> l1 <> l2 e. all2 S $;

theorem all2ss (R S: set): $ R C_ S -> all2 R C_ all2 S $;

theorem all2eqg (R S: set) (l1 l2: nat) {x y: nat}: $ A. x A. y (x IN l1 /\ y IN l2 -> (x <> y e. R <-> x <> y e. S)) -> (l1 <> l2 e. all2 R <-> l1 <> l2 e. all2 S) $;

theorem all2len (R: set) (l1 l2: nat): $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 R -> len l1 = len l2 $;

theorem all2i (G: wff) (R: set) (a b l1 l2 n: nat): $ G -> nth n l1 = suc a $ > $ G -> nth n l2 = suc b $ > $ G -> l1 <> l2 e. all2 R $ > $ G -> a <> b e. R $;

theorem all2com (R: set) (l1 l2: nat): $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 (cnv R) <-> l2 <> l1 e. all2 R $;

theorem all2cnv (R: set): $ all2 (cnv R) == cnv (all2 R) $;

theorem all20 (R: set): $ 0 <> 0 e. all2 R $;

theorem all201 (R: set) (l: nat): $ 0 <> l e. all2 R <-> l = 0 $;

theorem all202 (R: set) (l: nat): $ l <> 0 e. all2 R <-> l = 0 $;

theorem all2S (R: set) (a b l1 l2: nat): $ a : l1 <> b : l2 e. all2 R <-> a <> b e. R /\ l1 <> l2 e. all2 R $;

theorem all2S1 (R: set) (a: nat) {b: nat} (l1 l2: nat) {l2_: nat}: $ a : l1 <> l2 e. all2 R <-> E. b E. l2_ (l2 = b : l2_ /\ (a <> b e. R /\ l1 <> l2_ e. all2 R)) $;

theorem all2all2 (A: set) (l1 l2: nat) {x: nat}: $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 (S\ x, A) -> all A l2 $;

theorem all2all1 (A: set) (l1 l2: nat) {x y: nat}: $ l1 <> l2 e. all2 (S\ x, {y | x e. A}) -> all A l1 $;

local def rlrec (z: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): nat;

theorem rlreceqd (_G: wff) (_z1 _z2: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ > $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> rlrec _z1 _S1 _n1 = rlrec _z2 _S2 _n2 $;

theorem rlreceq (_z1 _z2: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _z1 = _z2 -> _S1 == _S2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> rlrec _z1 _S1 _n1 = rlrec _z2 _S2 _n2 $;

theorem rlreceq1d (_G: wff) (_z1 _z2: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _z1 = _z2 $ > $ _G -> rlrec _z1 S n = rlrec _z2 S n $;

theorem rlreceq1 (_z1 _z2: nat) (S: set) (n: nat): $ _z1 = _z2 -> rlrec _z1 S n = rlrec _z2 S n $;

theorem rlreceq2d (_G: wff) (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _G -> _S1 == _S2 $ > $ _G -> rlrec z _S1 n = rlrec z _S2 n $;

theorem rlreceq2 (z: nat) (_S1 _S2: set) (n: nat): $ _S1 == _S2 -> rlrec z _S1 n = rlrec z _S2 n $;

theorem rlreceq3d (_G: wff) (z: nat) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> rlrec z S _n1 = rlrec z S _n2 $;

theorem rlreceq3 (z: nat) (S: set) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> rlrec z S _n1 = rlrec z S _n2 $;

theorem rlrec0 (S: set) (z: nat): $ rlrec z S 0 = z $;

theorem rlrecS (S: set) (a l z: nat): $ rlrec z S (l |> a) = S @ (l <> a <> rlrec z S l) $;

theorem rlistindd (G: wff) {x l a: nat} (n: nat) (px: wff x) (p0 pn: wff) (pl: wff l) (ps: wff l a):
  $ x = n -> (px <-> pn) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = l -> (px <-> pl) $ >
  $ x = l |> a -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ G -> p0 $ >
  $ G /\ pl -> ps $ >
  $ G -> pn $;

theorem rlistind {x l a: nat} (n: nat) (px: wff x) (p0 pn: wff) (pl: wff l) (ps: wff l a):
  $ x = n -> (px <-> pn) $ >
  $ x = 0 -> (px <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = l -> (px <-> pl) $ >
  $ x = l |> a -> (px <-> ps) $ >
  $ p0 $ >
  $ pl -> ps $ >
  $ pn $;

def bit (n i: nat): nat;

theorem bitAndeq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitAnd a _b1 = bitAnd a _b2 $;

theorem bitAndeq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> bitAnd a _b1 = bitAnd a _b2 $;

pub theorem bitAndEq (a b: nat): $ ns (bitAnd a b) == ns a i^i ns b $;

theorem elbitAnd (a b i: nat): $ i e. ns (bitAnd a b) <-> i e. ns a /\ i e. ns b $;

theorem bitAnd_sym (a b: nat): $ bitAnd a b = bitAnd b a $;

theorem bitAnd_ass (a b c: nat): $ bitAnd (bitAnd a b) c = bitAnd a (bitAnd b c) $;

theorem bitAnd01 (a: nat): $ bitAnd 0 a = 0 $;

theorem bitAnd02 (a: nat): $ bitAnd a 0 = 0 $;

theorem bitAnd_idm (a: nat): $ bitAnd a a = a $;

theorem bitAndb0l (a b: nat): $ bitAnd (b0 a) b = b0 (bitAnd a (b // 2)) $;

theorem bitAndb0r (a b: nat): $ bitAnd a (b0 b) = b0 (bitAnd (a // 2) b) $;

theorem bitAndb00 (a b: nat): $ bitAnd (b0 a) (b0 b) = b0 (bitAnd a b) $;

theorem bitAndb01 (a b: nat): $ bitAnd (b0 a) (b1 b) = b0 (bitAnd a b) $;

theorem bitAndb10 (a b: nat): $ bitAnd (b1 a) (b0 b) = b0 (bitAnd a b) $;

theorem bitAndb11 (a b: nat): $ bitAnd (b1 a) (b1 b) = b1 (bitAnd a b) $;

abstract def bitOr (a b: nat): nat;

theorem bitOreqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitOr _a1 _b1 = bitOr _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitOreq (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> bitOr _a1 _b1 = bitOr _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitOreq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> bitOr _a1 b = bitOr _a2 b $;

theorem bitOreq1 (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> bitOr _a1 b = bitOr _a2 b $;

theorem bitOreq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitOr a _b1 = bitOr a _b2 $;

theorem bitOreq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> bitOr a _b1 = bitOr a _b2 $;

pub theorem bitOrEq (a b: nat): $ ns (bitOr a b) == ns a u. ns b $;

theorem elbitOr (a b i: nat): $ i e. ns (bitOr a b) <-> i e. ns a \/ i e. ns b $;

theorem bitOr_sym (a b: nat): $ bitOr a b = bitOr b a $;

theorem bitOr_ass (a b c: nat): $ bitOr (bitOr a b) c = bitOr a (bitOr b c) $;

theorem bitAnd_di (a b c: nat): $ bitAnd a (bitOr b c) = bitOr (bitAnd a b) (bitAnd a c) $;

theorem bitOr01 (a: nat): $ bitOr 0 a = a $;

theorem bitOr02 (a: nat): $ bitOr a 0 = a $;

theorem bitOr_idm (a: nat): $ bitOr a a = a $;

theorem bitOrb1l (a b: nat): $ bitOr (b1 a) b = b1 (bitOr a (b // 2)) $;

theorem bitOrb1r (a b: nat): $ bitOr a (b1 b) = b1 (bitOr (a // 2) b) $;

theorem bitOrb00 (a b: nat): $ bitOr (b0 a) (b0 b) = b0 (bitOr a b) $;

theorem bitOrb01 (a b: nat): $ bitOr (b0 a) (b1 b) = b1 (bitOr a b) $;

theorem bitOrb10 (a b: nat): $ bitOr (b1 a) (b0 b) = b1 (bitOr a b) $;

theorem bitOrb11 (a b: nat): $ bitOr (b1 a) (b1 b) = b1 (bitOr a b) $;

theorem bitAnd_add_bitOr (a b: nat): $ bitAnd a b + bitOr a b = a + b $;

theorem bitOr_eq_add2 (a b: nat): $ bitAnd a b = 0 -> bitOr a b = a + b $;

theorem bitOr_eq_add (a b: nat): $ ns a i^i ns b == ns 0 -> bitOr a b = a + b $;

abstract def bitDif (a b: nat): nat;

theorem bitDifeqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitDif _a1 _b1 = bitDif _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitDifeq (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> bitDif _a1 _b1 = bitDif _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitDifeq1d (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> bitDif _a1 b = bitDif _a2 b $;

theorem bitDifeq1 (_a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> bitDif _a1 b = bitDif _a2 b $;

theorem bitDifeq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitDif a _b1 = bitDif a _b2 $;

theorem bitDifeq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> bitDif a _b1 = bitDif a _b2 $;

theorem elbitDif (a b i: nat): $ i e. ns (bitDif a b) <-> i e. ns a /\ ~i e. ns b $;

theorem bitDif01 (a: nat): $ bitDif 0 a = 0 $;

theorem bitDif02 (a: nat): $ bitDif a 0 = a $;

theorem bitDifid (a: nat): $ bitDif a a = 0 $;

theorem bitDifeq0 (a b: nat): $ bitDif a b = 0 <-> ns a C_ ns b $;

theorem bitDifAndss (a b c: nat): $ ns a C_ ns c -> bitDif a (bitAnd c b) = bitDif a b $;

theorem bitDifAndid (a b: nat): $ bitDif a (bitAnd a b) = bitDif a b $;

theorem bitDifAnd (a b c: nat): $ bitDif (bitAnd a b) c = bitAnd a (bitDif b c) $;

theorem bitDifadd (a b: nat): $ ns b C_ ns a -> bitDif a b + b = a $;

theorem bitDifsub (a b: nat): $ ns b C_ ns a -> bitDif a b = a - b $;

abstract def bitXor (a b: nat): nat;

theorem bitXoreqd (_G: wff) (_a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitXor _a1 _b1 = bitXor _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitXoreq2d (_G: wff) (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitXor a _b1 = bitXor a _b2 $;

theorem bitXoreq2 (a _b1 _b2: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> bitXor a _b1 = bitXor a _b2 $;

def Bits (k: nat): nat;

theorem Bitseqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> Bits _k1 = Bits _k2 $;

theorem Bitseq (_k1 _k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> Bits _k1 = Bits _k2 $;

theorem Bitsle (m n v: nat): $ m <= n -> v e. ns (Bits m) -> v e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem Bitsss (m n: nat): $ m <= n -> ns (Bits m) C_ ns (Bits n) $;

theorem Bits_eq_power (n: nat): $ Bits n = power (upto n) $;

theorem elBits (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) <-> ns a C_ ns (upto n) $;

theorem elBits2 (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) <-> a < 2 ^ n $;

theorem elBitsS_el (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits (suc n)) -> (a e. ns (Bits n) <-> ~n e. ns a) $;

theorem uptoT (n: nat): $ upto n e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem elBits8mul (k n: nat): $ n e. ns (Bits (8 * k)) <-> n < 256 ^ k $;

theorem Bitsle1 (n v w: nat): $ v <= w -> w e. ns (Bits n) -> v e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem Bits_mod (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) -> a % 2 ^ n = a $;

theorem Bits_eqm (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) /\ b e. ns (Bits n) -> (mod(2 ^ n): a = b <-> a = b) $;

theorem Bits_zeqm (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) /\ b e. ns (Bits n) -> (modZ(2 ^ n): b0 a = b0 b <-> a = b) $;

theorem elBits0 (a: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits 0) <-> a = 0 $;

theorem elBits01 (n: nat): $ 0 e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem elBitsx01 (n: nat): $ h2n (x0) e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem elBits1 (a: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits 1) <-> bool a $;

theorem elBits11 (n: nat): $ 1 e. ns (Bits n) <-> n != 0 $;

theorem eq_bitAnd1 (a b: nat): $ ns a C_ ns b <-> bitAnd a b = a $;

theorem eq_bitAnd2 (a b: nat): $ ns a C_ ns b <-> bitAnd b a = a $;

theorem bitAndT1 (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) -> bitAnd a b e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem bitAndT2 (a b n: nat): $ b e. ns (Bits n) -> bitAnd a b e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem bitOrT (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) /\ b e. ns (Bits n) <-> bitOr a b e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem bitDifT (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) -> bitDif a b e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem mulBitsT (a b m n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits m) /\ b e. ns (Bits n) -> a * b e. ns (Bits (m + n)) $;

theorem shladdT (a b c n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) /\ c e. ns (Bits b) -> shl a b + c e. ns (Bits (n + b)) $;

theorem shlT (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) -> shl a b e. ns (Bits (n + b)) $;

theorem shlT2 (a b c n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) -> n + b <= c -> shl a b e. ns (Bits c) $;

theorem shrT (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits (n + b)) -> shr a b e. ns (Bits n) $;

theorem b1Bits (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) <-> b1 a e. ns (Bits (suc n)) $;

theorem b0Bits (a n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) <-> b0 a e. ns (Bits (suc n)) $;

theorem mod_el_Bits (a k: nat): $ a % 2 ^ k e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem h2nT (h: hex): $ h2n h e. ns (Bits 4) $;

theorem hexT (a k: nat) (x: hex): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> a :x x e. ns (Bits (k + 4)) $;

theorem hex2T (a k: nat) (x y: hex): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> a :x x :x y e. ns (Bits (k + 8)) $;

def chop (k n: nat): nat;

theorem chopeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> chop _k1 _n1 = chop _k2 _n2 $;

theorem chopeq (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> chop _k1 _n1 = chop _k2 _n2 $;

theorem chopeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> chop _k1 n = chop _k2 n $;

theorem chopeq1 (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> chop _k1 n = chop _k2 n $;

theorem chopeq2d (_G: wff) (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> chop k _n1 = chop k _n2 $;

theorem chopeq2 (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> chop k _n1 = chop k _n2 $;

pub theorem chopT (k n: nat): $ chop k n e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem el_chop (a k n: nat): $ a e. ns (chop k n) <-> a < k /\ a e. ns n $;

theorem bitAnd_upto (a k: nat): $ bitAnd (upto k) a = chop k a $;

theorem chop_upto (k m: nat): $ m <= k <-> chop m (upto k) = upto m $;

theorem shlshr_chop (k n: nat): $ shl (shr n k) k + chop k n = n $;

theorem chop_shl_0 (a k m: nat): $ m <= k -> chop m (shl a k) = 0 $;

theorem shladd_uniq (a k m n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) /\ shl m k + a = n <-> shr n k = m /\ chop k n = a $;

theorem chop_shladd (a b k: nat): $ b e. ns (Bits k) -> chop k (shl a k + b) = b $;

theorem chop4hex (a: nat) (b: hex): $ chop 4 (a :x b) = h2n b $;

theorem Bits_chop (a k: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> chop k a = a $;

theorem eqm_chop (a k: nat): $ mod(2 ^ k): chop k a = a $;

theorem chop_eq_chop (a b k: nat): $ chop k a = chop k b <-> mod(2 ^ k): a = b $;

theorem chop_chop (a m n: nat): $ m <= n -> chop m (chop n a) = chop m a $;

theorem chop_shl (a k n: nat): $ shl (chop n a) k = chop (n + k) (shl a k) $;

theorem chop_shr (a k n: nat): $ shr (chop (n + k) a) k = chop n (shr a k) $;

theorem chop_bitAnd1 (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitAnd a b) = bitAnd (chop m a) b $;

theorem chop_bitAnd2 (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitAnd a b) = bitAnd a (chop m b) $;

theorem chop_bitAnd (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitAnd a b) = bitAnd (chop m a) (chop m b) $;

theorem chop_bitOr (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitOr a b) = bitOr (chop m a) (chop m b) $;

theorem chop_bitDif1 (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitDif a b) = bitDif (chop m a) b $;

theorem chop_bitDif (a b m: nat): $ chop m (bitDif a b) = bitDif (chop m a) (chop m b) $;

theorem shl_bitAnd (a b m: nat): $ shl (bitAnd a b) m = bitAnd (shl a m) (shl b m) $;

theorem shl_bitOr (a b m: nat): $ shl (bitOr a b) m = bitOr (shl a m) (shl b m) $;

theorem shl_bitDif (a b m: nat): $ shl (bitDif a b) m = bitDif (shl a m) (shl b m) $;

theorem shr_bitAnd (a b m: nat): $ shr (bitAnd a b) m = bitAnd (shr a m) (shr b m) $;

theorem shr_bitOr (a b m: nat): $ shr (bitOr a b) m = bitOr (shr a m) (shr b m) $;

theorem shr_bitDif (a b m: nat): $ shr (bitDif a b) m = bitDif (shr a m) (shr b m) $;

theorem eqm_chopd (G: wff) (a b k: nat): $ G -> mod(2 ^ k): a = b $ > $ G -> mod(2 ^ k): chop k a = b $;

theorem zeqm_chopd (G: wff) (a b k: nat): $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): b0 a = b $ > $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (chop k a) = b $;

local def chopZ (k n: nat): nat;

theorem chopZeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> chopZ _k1 _n1 = chopZ _k2 _n2 $;

theorem chopZeq (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> chopZ _k1 _n1 = chopZ _k2 _n2 $;

theorem chopZeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> chopZ _k1 n = chopZ _k2 n $;

theorem chopZeq1 (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> chopZ _k1 n = chopZ _k2 n $;

theorem chopZeq2d (_G: wff) (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> chopZ k _n1 = chopZ k _n2 $;

theorem chopZeq2 (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> chopZ k _n1 = chopZ k _n2 $;

theorem chopZT (k n: nat): $ chopZ k n e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem chopZ_b0 (a k: nat): $ chopZ k (b0 a) = chop k a $;

theorem zeqm_chopZ (a k: nat): $ modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (chopZ k a) = a $;

theorem zeqm_chopZd (G: wff) (a b k: nat): $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): a = b $ > $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (chopZ k a) = b $;

theorem chopZ_eq_chopZ (a b k: nat): $ chopZ k a = chopZ k b <-> modZ(2 ^ k): a = b $;

theorem chopZ_b1 (a k: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> chopZ k (b1 a) = 2 ^ k - suc a $;

theorem chopZ_b1_2 (a k: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> chopZ k (b1 a) + suc a = 2 ^ k $;

theorem hex_divmod256 (a: nat) (b c: hex): $ a :x b :x c // 256 = a /\ a :x b :x c % 256 = h2n b :x c $;

theorem xchopshr8 (a: nat) (b c: hex): $ shr (a :x b :x c) 8 = a /\ chop 8 (a :x b :x c) = h2n b :x c $;

theorem s2nT (s: string): $ s2n s e. List (ns (u8)) $;

def bitsMSB (k n: nat): wff;

theorem bitsMSBeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (bitsMSB _k1 _n1 <-> bitsMSB _k2 _n2) $;

theorem bitsMSBeq (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> (bitsMSB _k1 _n1 <-> bitsMSB _k2 _n2) $;

theorem bitsMSBeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (bitsMSB _k1 n <-> bitsMSB _k2 n) $;

theorem bitsMSBeq1 (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (bitsMSB _k1 n <-> bitsMSB _k2 n) $;

theorem bitsMSBeq2d (_G: wff) (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (bitsMSB k _n1 <-> bitsMSB k _n2) $;

theorem bitsMSBeq2 (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> (bitsMSB k _n1 <-> bitsMSB k _n2) $;

theorem bitsMSB_b0 (k n: nat): $ bitsMSB k n <-> k e. ns (b0 n) $;

theorem bitsMSB_Bits (k n: nat): $ n e. ns (Bits k) -> (bitsMSB k n <-> ~n e. ns (Bits (k - 1))) $;

theorem bitsMSB_le (k n: nat): $ n e. ns (Bits k) -> (bitsMSB k n <-> 2 ^ (k - 1) <= n) $;

theorem chopZ_MSB (a k: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> (bitsMSB k (chopZ k a) <-> odd a) $;

theorem Bits_zeqm2 (a b n: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits n) /\ b e. ns (Bits n) -> (modZ(2 ^ n): a = b <-> a = b) $;

def sExt (m n v: nat): nat;

theorem sExteqd (_G: wff) (_m1 _m2 _n1 _n2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> sExt _m1 _n1 _v1 = sExt _m2 _n2 _v2 $;

theorem sExteq (_m1 _m2 _n1 _n2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> sExt _m1 _n1 _v1 = sExt _m2 _n2 _v2 $;

theorem sExteq1d (_G: wff) (_m1 _m2 n v: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> sExt _m1 n v = sExt _m2 n v $;

theorem sExteq1 (_m1 _m2 n v: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> sExt _m1 n v = sExt _m2 n v $;

theorem sExteq2d (_G: wff) (m _n1 _n2 v: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> sExt m _n1 v = sExt m _n2 v $;

theorem sExteq2 (m _n1 _n2 v: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> sExt m _n1 v = sExt m _n2 v $;

theorem sExteq3d (_G: wff) (m n _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> sExt m n _v1 = sExt m n _v2 $;

theorem sExteq3 (m n _v1 _v2: nat): $ _v1 = _v2 -> sExt m n _v1 = sExt m n _v2 $;

def sExtq (n v: nat): nat;

theorem sExtqeqd (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> sExtq _n1 _v1 = sExtq _n2 _v2 $;

theorem sExtqeq (_n1 _n2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> sExtq _n1 _v1 = sExtq _n2 _v2 $;

theorem sExtqeq1 (_n1 _n2 v: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> sExtq _n1 v = sExtq _n2 v $;

theorem sExtqeq2d (_G: wff) (n _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> sExtq n _v1 = sExtq n _v2 $;

pub theorem sExtT (m n v: nat): $ m <= n /\ v e. ns (Bits m) -> sExt m n v e. ns (Bits n) $;

pub theorem sExtqT (n v: nat): $ n <= 64 /\ v e. ns (Bits n) -> sExtq n v e. ns (u64) $;

theorem sExt_chopZ (a m n: nat): $ m <= n /\ a e. ns (Bits m) -> sExt m n (chopZ m a) = chopZ n a $;

def bitsUpdate (k m a n: nat): nat;

theorem bitsUpdateeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ >
  $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ >
  $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ >
  $ _G -> bitsUpdate _k1 _m1 _a1 _n1 = bitsUpdate _k2 _m2 _a2 _n2 $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _a1 _a2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> _a1 = _a2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> bitsUpdate _k1 _m1 _a1 _n1 = bitsUpdate _k2 _m2 _a2 _n2 $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 m a n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> bitsUpdate _k1 m a n = bitsUpdate _k2 m a n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq1 (_k1 _k2 m a n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> bitsUpdate _k1 m a n = bitsUpdate _k2 m a n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq2d (_G: wff) (k _m1 _m2 a n: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> bitsUpdate k _m1 a n = bitsUpdate k _m2 a n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq2 (k _m1 _m2 a n: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> bitsUpdate k _m1 a n = bitsUpdate k _m2 a n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq3d (_G: wff) (k m _a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> bitsUpdate k m _a1 n = bitsUpdate k m _a2 n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq3 (k m _a1 _a2 n: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> bitsUpdate k m _a1 n = bitsUpdate k m _a2 n $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq4d (_G: wff) (k m a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> bitsUpdate k m a _n1 = bitsUpdate k m a _n2 $;

theorem bitsUpdateeq4 (k m a _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> bitsUpdate k m a _n1 = bitsUpdate k m a _n2 $;

pub theorem bitsUpdateT (k m l a n: nat): $ k + m <= l /\ a e. ns (Bits m) /\ n e. ns (Bits l) -> bitsUpdate k m a n e. ns (Bits l) $;

def bitsNot (k n: nat): nat;

theorem bitsNoteqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> bitsNot _k1 _n1 = bitsNot _k2 _n2 $;

theorem bitsNoteq (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> bitsNot _k1 _n1 = bitsNot _k2 _n2 $;

theorem bitsNoteq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> bitsNot _k1 n = bitsNot _k2 n $;

theorem bitsNoteq1 (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> bitsNot _k1 n = bitsNot _k2 n $;

theorem bitsNoteq2d (_G: wff) (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> bitsNot k _n1 = bitsNot k _n2 $;

theorem bitsNoteq2 (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> bitsNot k _n1 = bitsNot k _n2 $;

pub theorem bitsNot_mem (k n i: nat): $ i e. ns (bitsNot k n) <-> i < k /\ ~i e. ns n $;

pub theorem bitsNotT (k n: nat): $ bitsNot k n e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem bitsNot_chop (k n: nat): $ bitsNot k (chop k n) = bitsNot k n $;

theorem bitsNot_add (k n: nat): $ n e. ns (Bits k) -> bitsNot k n + n = upto k $;

theorem bitsNot_sub (k n: nat): $ n e. ns (Bits k) -> bitsNot k n = upto k - n $;

theorem bitsNot0 (k: nat): $ bitsNot k 0 = upto k $;

theorem bitsNot01 (n: nat): $ bitsNot 0 n = 0 $;

theorem chop_bitsNot (k m n: nat): $ m <= k -> chop m (bitsNot k n) = bitsNot m n $;

theorem shl_bitsNot (a k m: nat): $ shl (bitsNot k a) m + upto m = bitsNot (k + m) (shl a m) $;

theorem shr_bitsNot (a k m: nat): $ shr (bitsNot k a) m = bitsNot (k - m) (shr a m) $;

theorem zeqm_bitsNot (k n: nat): $ modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (bitsNot k n) = -uZ b0 (suc n) $;

theorem zeqm_bitsNot2 (k n: nat): $ modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (bitsNot k n) = b1 n $;

theorem chopZ_b1_bitsNot (k n: nat): $ chopZ k (b1 n) = bitsNot k n $;

theorem zeqm_bitsNotd (G: wff) (a k x: nat): $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): b0 a = x $ > $ G -> modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (bitsNot k a) = -uZ (x +Z b0 1) $;

theorem bitsNot4_h2n (a: hex): $ bitsNot 4 (h2n a) + h2n a = h2n (xf) $;

theorem bitsNot4_hex (a: nat) (b: hex): $ bitsNot 4 (a :x b) + h2n b = h2n (xf) $;

theorem bitsNot_hex (a: nat) (b c: hex) (k: nat): $ h2n b + h2n c = h2n (xf) -> bitsNot (k + 4) (a :x b) = bitsNot k a :x c $;

theorem bitsAddeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _a1 _a2 _b1 _b2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> bitsAdd _k1 _a1 _b1 = bitsAdd _k2 _a2 _b2 $;

theorem bitsAddeq2d (_G: wff) (k _a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> bitsAdd k _a1 b = bitsAdd k _a2 b $;

theorem bitsAddeq2 (k _a1 _a2 b: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> bitsAdd k _a1 b = bitsAdd k _a2 b $;

pub theorem bitsAddT (k a b: nat): $ bitsAdd k a b e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem bitsAdd_eqid (a b k: nat): $ a + b e. ns (Bits k) -> bitsAdd k a b = a + b $;

theorem eqm_bitsAdd (a b k: nat): $ mod(2 ^ k): bitsAdd k a b = a + b $;

theorem zeqm_bitsAdd (a b k: nat): $ modZ(2 ^ k): b0 (bitsAdd k a b) = b0 a +Z b0 b $;

theorem eqm_bitsAddd (G: wff) (a b k x y: nat): $ G -> mod(2 ^ k): a = x $ > $ G -> mod(2 ^ k): b = y $ > $ G -> mod(2 ^ k): bitsAdd k a b = x + y $;

theorem toBytesAuxS {i: nat} (k n: nat): $ toBytesAux (suc k) n = \. i e. upto (suc n), (i % 256) : ns (toBytesAux k n) @ (i // 256) $;

theorem toBytesAuxS_app (a k n: nat): $ a <= n -> ns (toBytesAux (suc k) n) @ a = (a % 256) : ns (toBytesAux k n) @ (a // 256) $;

abstract def toBytes (k n: nat): nat;

theorem toByteseqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> toBytes _k1 _n1 = toBytes _k2 _n2 $;

theorem toByteseq (_k1 _k2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> toBytes _k1 _n1 = toBytes _k2 _n2 $;

theorem toByteseq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> toBytes _k1 n = toBytes _k2 n $;

theorem toByteseq1 (_k1 _k2 n: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> toBytes _k1 n = toBytes _k2 n $;

theorem toByteseq2d (_G: wff) (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> toBytes k _n1 = toBytes k _n2 $;

theorem toByteseq2 (k _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> toBytes k _n1 = toBytes k _n2 $;

pub theorem toBytes0 (n: nat): $ toBytes 0 n = 0 $;

theorem toBytesAuxS_eq (a k n: nat): $ a <= n -> ns (toBytesAux k n) @ a = toBytes k a $;

pub theorem toBytesS (k n: nat): $ toBytes (suc k) n = (n % 256) : toBytes k (n // 256) $;

theorem toBytesS2 (k n: nat): $ toBytes (suc k) n = chop 8 n : toBytes k (shr n 8) $;

theorem toBytes02 (k: nat): $ toBytes k 0 = repeat 0 k $;

pub theorem toBytesT (k n: nat): $ toBytes k n e. Array (ns (u8)) k $;

theorem toBytes1 (n: nat): $ toBytes 1 n = chop 8 n : 0 $;

theorem toBytes_chop (k n: nat): $ toBytes k (chop (8 * k) n) = toBytes k n $;

theorem toBytesS_bitsNot (k n: nat): $ toBytes (suc k) (bitsNot (8 * suc k) n) = bitsNot 8 n : toBytes k (bitsNot (8 * k) (shr n 8)) $;

theorem i64Byteseqd (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> i64Bytes _n1 = i64Bytes _n2 $;

theorem i64Byteseq (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> i64Bytes _n1 = i64Bytes _n2 $;

theorem i8Bytes_val2 (n: nat): $ i8Bytes n = toBytes 1 (chopZ 8 n) $;

theorem i16Bytes_val (n: nat): $ i16Bytes n = toBytes 2 (chopZ 16 n) $;

theorem i32Bytes_val (n: nat): $ i32Bytes n = toBytes 4 (chopZ 32 n) $;

theorem i64Bytes_val (n: nat): $ i64Bytes n = toBytes 8 (chopZ 64 n) $;

theorem i8Bytes_val (n: nat): $ i8Bytes n = chopZ 8 n : 0 $;

theorem toIBytesT (k n: nat): $ toIBytes k n e. Array (ns (u8)) k $;

theorem i8BytesT (n: nat): $ i8Bytes n e. Array (ns (u8)) 1 $;

theorem i16BytesT (n: nat): $ i16Bytes n e. Array (ns (u8)) 2 $;

theorem i32BytesT (n: nat): $ i32Bytes n e. Array (ns (u8)) 4 $;

theorem i64BytesT (n: nat): $ i64Bytes n e. Array (ns (u8)) 8 $;

theorem toIBytes0 (n: nat): $ toIBytes 0 n = 0 $;

theorem toIBytes_b0 (k n: nat): $ toIBytes k (b0 n) = toBytes k n $;

theorem toIBytesS_b1 (k n: nat): $ toIBytes (suc k) (b1 n) = bitsNot 8 n : toIBytes k (b1 (shr n 8)) $;

def Bitvec: set;

theorem elBitvec (bs n: nat): $ n <> bs e. Bitvec <-> bs < 2 ^ n $;

theorem elBitvec2 (bs n: nat): $ n <> bs e. Bitvec <-> bs e. ns (Bits n) $;

abstract def bvSize (bs: nat): nat;

theorem bvSizeeqd (_G: wff) (_bs1 _bs2: nat): $ _G -> _bs1 = _bs2 $ > $ _G -> bvSize _bs1 = bvSize _bs2 $;

theorem bvSizeeq (_bs1 _bs2: nat): $ _bs1 = _bs2 -> bvSize _bs1 = bvSize _bs2 $;

pub theorem bvSize0: $ bvSize 0 = 0 $;

pub theorem bvSizeS (k bs n: nat): $ bvSize ((k <> bs) : n) = k + bvSize n $;

theorem bvSize1 (bs k: nat): $ bvSize ((k <> bs) : 0) = k $;

theorem bvSizeA (bs1 bs2: nat): $ bvSize (bs1 ++ bs2) = bvSize bs1 + bvSize bs2 $;

def isBitvecs (bs k: nat): wff;

theorem isBitvecseqd (_G: wff) (_bs1 _bs2 _k1 _k2: nat): $ _G -> _bs1 = _bs2 $ > $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (isBitvecs _bs1 _k1 <-> isBitvecs _bs2 _k2) $;

theorem isBitvecseq (_bs1 _bs2 _k1 _k2: nat): $ _bs1 = _bs2 -> _k1 = _k2 -> (isBitvecs _bs1 _k1 <-> isBitvecs _bs2 _k2) $;

theorem isBitvecseq1d (_G: wff) (_bs1 _bs2 k: nat): $ _G -> _bs1 = _bs2 $ > $ _G -> (isBitvecs _bs1 k <-> isBitvecs _bs2 k) $;

theorem isBitvecseq1 (_bs1 _bs2 k: nat): $ _bs1 = _bs2 -> (isBitvecs _bs1 k <-> isBitvecs _bs2 k) $;

theorem isBitvecseq2d (_G: wff) (bs _k1 _k2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (isBitvecs bs _k1 <-> isBitvecs bs _k2) $;

theorem isBitvecseq2 (bs _k1 _k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (isBitvecs bs _k1 <-> isBitvecs bs _k2) $;

abstract def ofBits (n: nat): nat;

theorem ofBitseqd (_G: wff) (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> ofBits _n1 = ofBits _n2 $;

theorem ofBitseq (_n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> ofBits _n1 = ofBits _n2 $;

pub theorem ofBits0: $ ofBits 0 = 0 $;

pub theorem ofBitsS (k bs n: nat): $ ofBits ((k <> bs) : n) = bs + shl (ofBits n) k $;

theorem ofBitsS2 (bs k n: nat): $ ofBits ((k <> bs) : n) = shl (ofBits n) k + bs $;

theorem ofBits1 (bs k: nat): $ ofBits ((k <> bs) : 0) = bs $;

pub theorem ofBits0T: $ ofBits 0 e. ns (Bits 0) $;

pub theorem ofBitsST (k bs n m: nat): $ bs e. ns (Bits k) /\ ofBits n e. ns (Bits m) -> ofBits ((k <> bs) : n) e. ns (Bits (k + m)) $;

theorem ofBitsT (bs: nat): $ bs e. List (Bitvec) -> ofBits bs e. ns (Bits (bvSize bs)) $;

theorem ofBitsA (bs1 bs2: nat): $ ofBits (bs1 ++ bs2) = shl (ofBits bs2) (bvSize bs1) + ofBits bs1 $;

def splitBits (bs n: nat): wff;

theorem splitBitseqd (_G: wff) (_bs1 _bs2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _bs1 = _bs2 $ > $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (splitBits _bs1 _n1 <-> splitBits _bs2 _n2) $;

theorem splitBitseq (_bs1 _bs2 _n1 _n2: nat): $ _bs1 = _bs2 -> _n1 = _n2 -> (splitBits _bs1 _n1 <-> splitBits _bs2 _n2) $;

theorem splitBitseq1d (_G: wff) (_bs1 _bs2 n: nat): $ _G -> _bs1 = _bs2 $ > $ _G -> (splitBits _bs1 n <-> splitBits _bs2 n) $;

theorem splitBitseq1 (_bs1 _bs2 n: nat): $ _bs1 = _bs2 -> (splitBits _bs1 n <-> splitBits _bs2 n) $;

theorem splitBitseq2d (_G: wff) (bs _n1 _n2: nat): $ _G -> _n1 = _n2 $ > $ _G -> (splitBits bs _n1 <-> splitBits bs _n2) $;

theorem splitBitseq2 (bs _n1 _n2: nat): $ _n1 = _n2 -> (splitBits bs _n1 <-> splitBits bs _n2) $;

pub theorem splitBitsT (bs n k: nat): $ isBitvecs bs k /\ splitBits bs n -> n e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem splitBitsTi (bs k n: nat): $ bvSize bs = k $ > $ splitBits bs n -> n e. ns (Bits k) $;

theorem splitBits0 (n: nat): $ splitBits 0 n <-> n = 0 $;

theorem splitBitsS2 (a bs k n: nat): $ splitBits ((k <> a) : bs) n <-> a e. ns (Bits k) /\ bs e. List (Bitvec) /\ shl (ofBits bs) k + a = n $;

theorem splitBitsS (a bs k: nat) {m: nat} (n: nat): $ splitBits ((k <> a) : bs) n <-> a e. ns (Bits k) /\ E. m (shl m k + a = n /\ splitBits bs m) $;

theorem splitBits1 (a k n: nat): $ splitBits ((k <> a) : 0) n <-> a e. ns (Bits k) /\ a = n $;

theorem splitBits1i (a k: nat): $ a e. ns (Bits k) -> splitBits ((k <> a) : 0) a $;

theorem splitBitsS_uniq (a bs k n: nat): $ splitBits ((k <> a) : bs) n <-> chop k n = a /\ splitBits bs (shr n k) $;

theorem splitBitsS4 (a: hex) (bs: nat) {m: nat} (n: nat): $ splitBits ((4 <> h2n a) : bs) n <-> E. m (m :x a = n /\ splitBits bs m) $;

theorem splitBitsA {a: nat} (bs1 bs2 k n: nat): $ bvSize bs1 = k -> (splitBits (bs1 ++ bs2) n <-> E. a (splitBits bs1 a /\ splitBits ((k <> a) : bs2) n)) $;

theorem splitBits_split {a: nat} (b bs: nat) {c: nat} (k l n: nat): $ splitBits ((k + l <> b) : bs) n <-> E. a E. c (shl c k + a = b /\ splitBits ((k <> a) : (l <> c) : bs) n) $;

theorem splitBits_mid {a: nat} (b bs1 bs2: nat) {c: nat} (k l n: nat): $ splitBits (bs1 ++ (k + l <> b) : bs2) n <-> E. a E. c (shl c k + a = b /\ splitBits (bs1 ++ (k <> a) : (l <> c) : bs2) n) $;

theorem readModRM2eq (_rex1 _rex2 _rm1 _rm2 _rm21 _rm22 _mod1 _mod2 _l1 _l2: nat):

  $ readModRM rex rn rm l <-> E. b E. rm2 E. opc E. m (splitBits ((3 <> rm2) : (3 <> opc) : (2 <> m) : 0) b /\ rn = rex_reg (REX_R rex) opc /\ E. l2 (l = b : l2 /\ readModRM2 rex rm rm2 m l2)) $;

def opSize (have_rex: wff) (w v: nat): nat;

theorem opSizeeqd (_G _have_rex1 _have_rex2: wff) (_w1 _w2 _v1 _v2: nat):
  $ _G -> (_have_rex1 <-> _have_rex2) $ >
  $ _G -> _w1 = _w2 $ >
  $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ >
  $ _G -> opSize _have_rex1 _w1 _v1 = opSize _have_rex2 _w2 _v2 $;

theorem opSizeeq (_have_rex1 _have_rex2: wff) (_w1 _w2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ (_have_rex1 <-> _have_rex2) -> _w1 = _w2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> opSize _have_rex1 _w1 _v1 = opSize _have_rex2 _w2 _v2 $;

theorem opSizeeq1d (_G _have_rex1 _have_rex2: wff) (w v: nat): $ _G -> (_have_rex1 <-> _have_rex2) $ > $ _G -> opSize _have_rex1 w v = opSize _have_rex2 w v $;

theorem opSizeeq1 (_have_rex1 _have_rex2: wff) (w v: nat): $ (_have_rex1 <-> _have_rex2) -> opSize _have_rex1 w v = opSize _have_rex2 w v $;

theorem opSizeeq2d (_G have_rex: wff) (_w1 _w2 v: nat): $ _G -> _w1 = _w2 $ > $ _G -> opSize have_rex _w1 v = opSize have_rex _w2 v $;

theorem opSizeeq2 (have_rex: wff) (_w1 _w2 v: nat): $ _w1 = _w2 -> opSize have_rex _w1 v = opSize have_rex _w2 v $;

theorem opSizeeq3d (_G have_rex: wff) (w _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> opSize have_rex w _v1 = opSize have_rex w _v2 $;

theorem opSizeeq3 (have_rex: wff) (w _v1 _v2: nat): $ _v1 = _v2 -> opSize have_rex w _v1 = opSize have_rex w _v2 $;

def opSizeW (rex v: nat): nat;

def R_rm (r rm: nat): nat;

def mkCfg (ex rip regs flags mem: nat): nat;

theorem mkCfgeqd (_G: wff) (_ex1 _ex2 _rip1 _rip2 _regs1 _regs2 _flags1 _flags2 _mem1 _mem2: nat):
  $ _G -> _ex1 = _ex2 $ >
  $ _G -> _rip1 = _rip2 $ >
  $ _G -> _regs1 = _regs2 $ >
  $ _G -> _flags1 = _flags2 $ >
  $ _G -> _mem1 = _mem2 $ >
  $ _G -> mkCfg _ex1 _rip1 _regs1 _flags1 _mem1 = mkCfg _ex2 _rip2 _regs2 _flags2 _mem2 $;

theorem mkCfgeq (_ex1 _ex2 _rip1 _rip2 _regs1 _regs2 _flags1 _flags2 _mem1 _mem2: nat):
  $ _ex1 = _ex2 -> _rip1 = _rip2 -> _regs1 = _regs2 -> _flags1 = _flags2 -> _mem1 = _mem2 -> mkCfg _ex1 _rip1 _regs1 _flags1 _mem1 = mkCfg _ex2 _rip2 _regs2 _flags2 _mem2 $;

theorem mkCfgeq1d (_G: wff) (_ex1 _ex2 rip regs flags mem: nat): $ _G -> _ex1 = _ex2 $ > $ _G -> mkCfg _ex1 rip regs flags mem = mkCfg _ex2 rip regs flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq1 (_ex1 _ex2 rip regs flags mem: nat): $ _ex1 = _ex2 -> mkCfg _ex1 rip regs flags mem = mkCfg _ex2 rip regs flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq2d (_G: wff) (ex _rip1 _rip2 regs flags mem: nat): $ _G -> _rip1 = _rip2 $ > $ _G -> mkCfg ex _rip1 regs flags mem = mkCfg ex _rip2 regs flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq2 (ex _rip1 _rip2 regs flags mem: nat): $ _rip1 = _rip2 -> mkCfg ex _rip1 regs flags mem = mkCfg ex _rip2 regs flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq3d (_G: wff) (ex rip _regs1 _regs2 flags mem: nat): $ _G -> _regs1 = _regs2 $ > $ _G -> mkCfg ex rip _regs1 flags mem = mkCfg ex rip _regs2 flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq3 (ex rip _regs1 _regs2 flags mem: nat): $ _regs1 = _regs2 -> mkCfg ex rip _regs1 flags mem = mkCfg ex rip _regs2 flags mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq4d (_G: wff) (ex rip regs _flags1 _flags2 mem: nat): $ _G -> _flags1 = _flags2 $ > $ _G -> mkCfg ex rip regs _flags1 mem = mkCfg ex rip regs _flags2 mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq4 (ex rip regs _flags1 _flags2 mem: nat): $ _flags1 = _flags2 -> mkCfg ex rip regs _flags1 mem = mkCfg ex rip regs _flags2 mem $;

theorem mkCfgeq5d (_G: wff) (ex rip regs flags _mem1 _mem2: nat): $ _G -> _mem1 = _mem2 $ > $ _G -> mkCfg ex rip regs flags _mem1 = mkCfg ex rip regs flags _mem2 $;

theorem mkCfgeq5 (ex rip regs flags _mem1 _mem2: nat): $ _mem1 = _mem2 -> mkCfg ex rip regs flags _mem1 = mkCfg ex rip regs flags _mem2 $;

pub theorem mkCfgT (ex rip regs flags mem: nat):
  $ mkCfg ex rip regs flags mem e. Config <-> ex e. Option (Exception) /\ rip e. ns (u64) /\ regs e. Arrow (ns (Regs)) (ns (u64)) /\ flags e. ns (Flags) /\ mem e. Memory $;

theorem mkCfg_ex {e f i: nat} (k: nat) {m rs: nat}: $ E. e E. i E. rs E. f E. m k = mkCfg e i rs f m $;

theorem writeMemeq4d (_G: wff) (k a l _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (writeMem k a l _k21 <-> writeMem k a l _k22) $;

theorem writeMemeq4 (k a l _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (writeMem k a l _k21 <-> writeMem k a l _k22) $;

pub theorem writeMemT (k a l k2: nat): $ writeMem k a l k2 -> k e. Config /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ l e. List (ns (u8)) /\ k2 e. Config $;

local def setMemory (k m: nat): nat;

theorem setMemoryeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> setMemory _k1 _m1 = setMemory _k2 _m2 $;

theorem setMemoryeq (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> setMemory _k1 _m1 = setMemory _k2 _m2 $;

theorem setMemoryeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 m: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> setMemory _k1 m = setMemory _k2 m $;

theorem setMemoryeq1 (_k1 _k2 m: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> setMemory _k1 m = setMemory _k2 m $;

theorem setMemoryeq2d (_G: wff) (k _m1 _m2: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> setMemory k _m1 = setMemory k _m2 $;

theorem setMemoryeq2 (k _m1 _m2: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> setMemory k _m1 = setMemory k _m2 $;

theorem setMemoryT (k m: nat): $ k e. Config /\ m e. Memory -> setMemory k m e. Config $;

theorem setMemory_mk (e f ip m m2 r: nat): $ setMemory (mkCfg e ip r f m) m2 = mkCfg e ip r f m2 $;

theorem readException_setMemory (k m: nat): $ readException (setMemory k m) = readException k $;

theorem readRIP_setMemory (k m: nat): $ readRIP (setMemory k m) = readRIP k $;

theorem readReg_setMemory (k m r: nat): $ readReg (setMemory k m) r = readReg k r $;

theorem readFlags_setMemory (k m: nat): $ readFlags (setMemory k m) = readFlags k $;

theorem get_setMemory (k m2: nat): $ getMemory (setMemory k m2) = m2 $;

theorem set_setMemory (k m2 m3: nat): $ setMemory (setMemory k m2) m3 = setMemory k m3 $;

abstract def readEA (k sz ea v: nat): wff;

theorem readEAeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _v1 _v2: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ >
  $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ >
  $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ >
  $ _G -> (readEA _k1 _sz1 _ea1 _v1 <-> readEA _k2 _sz2 _ea2 _v2) $;

theorem readEAeq (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _sz1 = _sz2 -> _ea1 = _ea2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> (readEA _k1 _sz1 _ea1 _v1 <-> readEA _k2 _sz2 _ea2 _v2) $;

theorem readEAeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 sz ea v: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA _k1 sz ea v <-> readEA _k2 sz ea v) $;

theorem readEAeq1 (_k1 _k2 sz ea v: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (readEA _k1 sz ea v <-> readEA _k2 sz ea v) $;

theorem readEAeq2d (_G: wff) (k _sz1 _sz2 ea v: nat): $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA k _sz1 ea v <-> readEA k _sz2 ea v) $;

theorem readEAeq2 (k _sz1 _sz2 ea v: nat): $ _sz1 = _sz2 -> (readEA k _sz1 ea v <-> readEA k _sz2 ea v) $;

theorem readEAeq3d (_G: wff) (k sz _ea1 _ea2 v: nat): $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA k sz _ea1 v <-> readEA k sz _ea2 v) $;

theorem readEAeq3 (k sz _ea1 _ea2 v: nat): $ _ea1 = _ea2 -> (readEA k sz _ea1 v <-> readEA k sz _ea2 v) $;

theorem readEAeq4d (_G: wff) (k sz ea _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA k sz ea _v1 <-> readEA k sz ea _v2) $;

theorem readEAeq4 (k sz ea _v1 _v2: nat): $ _v1 = _v2 -> (readEA k sz ea _v1 <-> readEA k sz ea _v2) $;

pub theorem readEA_i (k q sz v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ q e. ns (u64) /\ sz e. WSize -> (readEA k sz (EA_i q) v <-> v = chop (wsizeBits sz) q) $;

pub theorem readEA_r (k sz r v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ r e. ns (Regs) /\ sz e. WSize -> (readEA k sz (EA_r r) v <-> v = readRegSz k sz r) $;

pub theorem readEA_m (k a sz v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ sz e. WSize -> (readEA k sz (EA_m a) v <-> v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) /\ readMem k a (toBytes (wsizeBytes sz) v)) $;

pub theorem readEA_T (k sz ea v: nat): $ readEA k sz ea v -> k e. Config /\ ea e. EA /\ sz e. WSize /\ v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) $;

theorem readEA_T64 (k sz ea v: nat): $ readEA k sz ea v -> k e. Config /\ ea e. EA /\ sz e. WSize /\ v e. ns (u64) $;

def readEA64 (k ea v: nat): wff;

theorem readEA64eq (_k1 _k2 _ea1 _ea2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _ea1 = _ea2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> (readEA64 _k1 _ea1 _v1 <-> readEA64 _k2 _ea2 _v2) $;

theorem readEA64eq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 ea v: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA64 _k1 ea v <-> readEA64 _k2 ea v) $;

theorem readEA64eq1 (_k1 _k2 ea v: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (readEA64 _k1 ea v <-> readEA64 _k2 ea v) $;

theorem readEA64eq2d (_G: wff) (k _ea1 _ea2 v: nat): $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ > $ _G -> (readEA64 k _ea1 v <-> readEA64 k _ea2 v) $;
