def setException (k e: nat): nat;

theorem setExceptioneqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _e1 _e2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _e1 = _e2 $ > $ _G -> setException _k1 _e1 = setException _k2 _e2 $;

theorem setExceptioneq (_k1 _k2 _e1 _e2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _e1 = _e2 -> setException _k1 _e1 = setException _k2 _e2 $;

theorem setExceptioneq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 e: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> setException _k1 e = setException _k2 e $;

theorem setExceptioneq1 (_k1 _k2 e: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> setException _k1 e = setException _k2 e $;

theorem setExceptioneq2d (_G: wff) (k _e1 _e2: nat): $ _G -> _e1 = _e2 $ > $ _G -> setException k _e1 = setException k _e2 $;

theorem setExceptioneq2 (k _e1 _e2: nat): $ _e1 = _e2 -> setException k _e1 = setException k _e2 $;

pub theorem setExceptionVal (ex ip rs f m e: nat): $ setException (mkCfg ex ip rs f m) e = mkCfg e ip rs f m $;

pub theorem setExceptionT (k e: nat): $ k e. Config /\ e e. Option (Exception) -> setException k e e. Config $;

theorem getMem_setException (e k: nat): $ getMemory (setException k e) = getMemory k $;

theorem read_setException (k ex ip rs f m e: nat): $ readException (setException k e) = e $;

theorem writeMem_set {e m2: nat} (k a l k2: nat):
  $ writeMem k a l k2 <-> k e. Config /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ l e. List (ns (u8)) /\ readException k = 0 /\ E. m2 E. e (writeMemory (getMemory k) a l m2 e /\ k2 = setException (setMemory k m2) e) $;

abstract def setReg (k r q: nat): nat;

theorem setRegeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _r1 _r2 _q1 _q2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _r1 = _r2 $ > $ _G -> _q1 = _q2 $ > $ _G -> setReg _k1 _r1 _q1 = setReg _k2 _r2 _q2 $;

theorem setRegeq (_k1 _k2 _r1 _r2 _q1 _q2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _r1 = _r2 -> _q1 = _q2 -> setReg _k1 _r1 _q1 = setReg _k2 _r2 _q2 $;

theorem setRegeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 r q: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> setReg _k1 r q = setReg _k2 r q $;

theorem setRegeq1 (_k1 _k2 r q: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> setReg _k1 r q = setReg _k2 r q $;

theorem setRegeq2d (_G: wff) (k _r1 _r2 q: nat): $ _G -> _r1 = _r2 $ > $ _G -> setReg k _r1 q = setReg k _r2 q $;

theorem setRegeq2 (k _r1 _r2 q: nat): $ _r1 = _r2 -> setReg k _r1 q = setReg k _r2 q $;

theorem setRegeq3d (_G: wff) (k r _q1 _q2: nat): $ _G -> _q1 = _q2 $ > $ _G -> setReg k r _q1 = setReg k r _q2 $;

theorem setRegeq3 (k r _q1 _q2: nat): $ _q1 = _q2 -> setReg k r _q1 = setReg k r _q2 $;

pub theorem setRegVal (ex ip rs f m r q: nat): $ setReg (mkCfg ex ip rs f m) r q = mkCfg ex ip (lower (write (ns rs) r q)) f m $;

pub theorem setRegT (k r q: nat): $ k e. Config /\ r e. ns (Regs) /\ q e. ns (u64) -> setReg k r q e. Config $;

theorem setRegMem (k q r: nat): $ getMemory (setReg k r q) = getMemory k $;

abstract def writeReg (k sz r v: nat): nat;

theorem writeRegeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _r1 _r2 _v1 _v2: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ >
  $ _G -> _r1 = _r2 $ >
  $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ >
  $ _G -> writeReg _k1 _sz1 _r1 _v1 = writeReg _k2 _sz2 _r2 _v2 $;

theorem writeRegeq (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _r1 _r2 _v1 _v2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _sz1 = _sz2 -> _r1 = _r2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> writeReg _k1 _sz1 _r1 _v1 = writeReg _k2 _sz2 _r2 _v2 $;

theorem writeRegeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 sz r v: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> writeReg _k1 sz r v = writeReg _k2 sz r v $;

theorem writeRegeq1 (_k1 _k2 sz r v: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> writeReg _k1 sz r v = writeReg _k2 sz r v $;

theorem writeRegeq2d (_G: wff) (k _sz1 _sz2 r v: nat): $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ > $ _G -> writeReg k _sz1 r v = writeReg k _sz2 r v $;

theorem writeRegeq2 (k _sz1 _sz2 r v: nat): $ _sz1 = _sz2 -> writeReg k _sz1 r v = writeReg k _sz2 r v $;

theorem writeRegeq3d (_G: wff) (k sz _r1 _r2 v: nat): $ _G -> _r1 = _r2 $ > $ _G -> writeReg k sz _r1 v = writeReg k sz _r2 v $;

theorem writeRegeq3 (k sz _r1 _r2 v: nat): $ _r1 = _r2 -> writeReg k sz _r1 v = writeReg k sz _r2 v $;

theorem writeRegeq4d (_G: wff) (k sz r _v1 _v2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> writeReg k sz r _v1 = writeReg k sz r _v2 $;

theorem writeRegeq4 (k sz r _v1 _v2: nat): $ _v1 = _v2 -> writeReg k sz r _v1 = writeReg k sz r _v2 $;

pub theorem writeReg8 (k r v: nat) (have_rex: wff): $ writeReg k (wSz8 have_rex) r v = if (~have_rex /\ 2 e. ns r) (setReg k (r - 4) (bitsUpdate 8 8 v (readReg k (r - 4)))) (setReg k r (bitsUpdate 0 8 v (readReg k r))) $;

pub theorem writeReg16 (k r v: nat): $ writeReg k (wSz16) r v = setReg k r (bitsUpdate 0 16 v (readReg k r)) $;

theorem writeReg_gt (k r sz v: nat): $ 16 < wsizeBits sz -> writeReg k sz r v = setReg k r v $;

pub theorem writeReg32 (k r v: nat): $ writeReg k (wSz32) r v = setReg k r v $;

pub theorem writeReg64 (k r v: nat): $ writeReg k (wSz64) r v = setReg k r v $;

pub theorem writeRegT (k sz r v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ sz e. WSize /\ r e. ns (Regs) /\ v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) -> writeReg k sz r v e. Config $;

abstract def writeEASz (k sz ea v k2: nat): wff;

theorem writeEASzeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _v1 _v2 _k21 _k22: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ >
  $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ >
  $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ >
  $ _G -> (writeEASz _k1 _sz1 _ea1 _v1 _k21 <-> writeEASz _k2 _sz2 _ea2 _v2 _k22) $;

theorem writeEASzeq (_k1 _k2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _v1 _v2 _k21 _k22: nat):
  $ _k1 = _k2 -> _sz1 = _sz2 -> _ea1 = _ea2 -> _v1 = _v2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> (writeEASz _k1 _sz1 _ea1 _v1 _k21 <-> writeEASz _k2 _sz2 _ea2 _v2 _k22) $;

theorem writeEASzeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 sz ea v k2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (writeEASz _k1 sz ea v k2 <-> writeEASz _k2 sz ea v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq1 (_k1 _k2 sz ea v k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (writeEASz _k1 sz ea v k2 <-> writeEASz _k2 sz ea v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq2d (_G: wff) (k _sz1 _sz2 ea v k2: nat): $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ > $ _G -> (writeEASz k _sz1 ea v k2 <-> writeEASz k _sz2 ea v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq2 (k _sz1 _sz2 ea v k2: nat): $ _sz1 = _sz2 -> (writeEASz k _sz1 ea v k2 <-> writeEASz k _sz2 ea v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq3d (_G: wff) (k sz _ea1 _ea2 v k2: nat): $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ > $ _G -> (writeEASz k sz _ea1 v k2 <-> writeEASz k sz _ea2 v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq3 (k sz _ea1 _ea2 v k2: nat): $ _ea1 = _ea2 -> (writeEASz k sz _ea1 v k2 <-> writeEASz k sz _ea2 v k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq4d (_G: wff) (k sz ea _v1 _v2 k2: nat): $ _G -> _v1 = _v2 $ > $ _G -> (writeEASz k sz ea _v1 k2 <-> writeEASz k sz ea _v2 k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq4 (k sz ea _v1 _v2 k2: nat): $ _v1 = _v2 -> (writeEASz k sz ea _v1 k2 <-> writeEASz k sz ea _v2 k2) $;

theorem writeEASzeq5d (_G: wff) (k sz ea v _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (writeEASz k sz ea v _k21 <-> writeEASz k sz ea v _k22) $;

theorem writeEASzeq5 (k sz ea v _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (writeEASz k sz ea v _k21 <-> writeEASz k sz ea v _k22) $;

pub theorem writeEASz_i (k sz i v k2: nat): $ ~writeEASz k sz (EA_i i) v k2 $;

pub theorem writeEASz_r (k sz r v k2: nat): $ k e. Config /\ sz e. WSize /\ r e. ns (Regs) /\ v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) -> (writeEASz k sz (EA_r r) v k2 <-> k2 = writeReg k sz r v) $;

pub theorem writeEASz_m {l: nat} (k sz a v k2: nat): $ k e. Config /\ sz e. WSize /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) -> (writeEASz k sz (EA_m a) v k2 <-> writeMem k a (toBytes (wsizeBits sz) v) k2) $;

pub theorem writeEASzT (k sz ea v k2: nat): $ writeEASz k sz ea v k2 -> k e. Config /\ sz e. WSize /\ ea e. EA /\ v e. ns (Bits (wsizeBits sz)) /\ k2 e. Config $;

abstract def writeRIP (k q: nat): nat;

theorem writeRIPeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _q1 _q2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _q1 = _q2 $ > $ _G -> writeRIP _k1 _q1 = writeRIP _k2 _q2 $;

theorem writeRIPeq (_k1 _k2 _q1 _q2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _q1 = _q2 -> writeRIP _k1 _q1 = writeRIP _k2 _q2 $;

theorem EA_callDesteq1 (_k1 _k2 ea v: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (EA_callDest _k1 ea v <-> EA_callDest _k2 ea v) $;

pub theorem EA_callDest_i (k i v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ i e. ns (u64) -> (EA_callDest k (EA_i i) v <-> v = readRIP k +_64 i) $;

pub theorem EA_callDest_r (k r v: nat): $ k e. Config /\ r e. ns (Regs) -> (EA_callDest k (EA_r r) v <-> v = readReg k r) $;

theorem writeFlagseqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _f1 _f2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _f1 = _f2 $ > $ _G -> writeFlags _k1 _f1 = writeFlags _k2 _f2 $;

abstract def setCZSO (k: nat) (c z s o: wff): nat;

theorem setCZSOeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat) (_c1 _c2 _z1 _z2 _s1 _s2 _o1 _o2: wff):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> (_c1 <-> _c2) $ >
  $ _G -> (_z1 <-> _z2) $ >
  $ _G -> (_s1 <-> _s2) $ >
  $ _G -> (_o1 <-> _o2) $ >
  $ _G -> setCZSO _k1 _c1 _z1 _s1 _o1 = setCZSO _k2 _c2 _z2 _s2 _o2 $;

theorem setCZSOeq (_k1 _k2: nat) (_c1 _c2 _z1 _z2 _s1 _s2 _o1 _o2: wff): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (_c1 <-> _c2) -> (_z1 <-> _z2) -> (_s1 <-> _s2) -> (_o1 <-> _o2) -> setCZSO _k1 _c1 _z1 _s1 _o1 = setCZSO _k2 _c2 _z2 _s2 _o2 $;

theorem setCZSOeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat) (c z s o: wff): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> setCZSO _k1 c z s o = setCZSO _k2 c z s o $;

theorem setCZSOeq1 (_k1 _k2: nat) (c z s o: wff): $ _k1 = _k2 -> setCZSO _k1 c z s o = setCZSO _k2 c z s o $;

theorem setCZSOeq2d (_G: wff) (k: nat) (_c1 _c2 z s o: wff): $ _G -> (_c1 <-> _c2) $ > $ _G -> setCZSO k _c1 z s o = setCZSO k _c2 z s o $;

theorem setCZSOeq2 (k: nat) (_c1 _c2 z s o: wff): $ (_c1 <-> _c2) -> setCZSO k _c1 z s o = setCZSO k _c2 z s o $;

pub theorem writeBinopAdd {w c o: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopAdd) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. w E. c E. o (addCarry sz a b w c o /\ writeCFOFResult k sz ea w (true c) (true o) k2) $;

pub theorem writeBinopSub {w c o: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopSub) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. w E. c E. o (subBorrow sz a b w c o /\ writeCFOFResult k sz ea w (true c) (true o) k2) $;

pub theorem writeBinopCmp {w c o: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopCmp) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. w E. c E. o (subBorrow sz a b w c o /\ k2 = writeResultFlags k sz w (true c) (true o)) $;

pub theorem writeBinopTst (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopTst) sz ea a b k2 <-> k2 = writeResultFlags k sz (bitAnd a b) F. F. $;

pub theorem writeBinopAnd (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopAnd) sz ea a b k2 <-> writeCFOFResult k sz ea (bitAnd a b) F. F. k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopXor (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopXor) sz ea a b k2 <-> writeCFOFResult k sz ea (bitXor a b) F. F. k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopOr (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopOr) sz ea a b k2 <-> writeCFOFResult k sz ea (bitOr a b) F. F. k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopShl {k3: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopShl) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. k3 (eraseFlags k k3 /\ writeEA k3 sz ea (shl a (maskShift sz b)) k2) $;

pub theorem writeBinopShr {k3: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopShr) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. k3 (eraseFlags k k3 /\ writeEA k3 sz ea (shr a (maskShift sz b)) k2) $;

pub theorem writeBinopSar {k3: nat} (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ writeBinop k (binopSar) sz ea a b k2 <-> E. k3 (eraseFlags k k3 /\ writeEA k3 sz ea (bitsSar (wsizeBits sz) a (maskShift sz b)) k2) $;

pub theorem writeBinopAdc (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopAdc) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopSbb (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopSbb) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopRol (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopRol) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopRor (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopRor) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopRcl (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopRcl) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopRcr (k sz ea a b k2: nat): $ ~writeBinop k (binopRcr) sz ea a b k2 $;

pub theorem writeBinopT (k op sz ea a b k2: nat): $ k e. Config /\ op e. ns (Binop) /\ sz e. WSize /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ b e. ns (u64) /\ ea e. EA /\ writeBinop k op sz ea a b k2 -> k2 e. Config $;

abstract def writeUnop (k op sz ea a k2: nat): wff;

theorem writeUnopeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _op1 _op2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _a1 _a2 _k21 _k22: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _op1 = _op2 $ >
  $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ >
  $ _G -> _ea1 = _ea2 $ >
  $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ >
  $ _G -> (writeUnop _k1 _op1 _sz1 _ea1 _a1 _k21 <-> writeUnop _k2 _op2 _sz2 _ea2 _a2 _k22) $;

theorem writeUnopeq (_k1 _k2 _op1 _op2 _sz1 _sz2 _ea1 _ea2 _a1 _a2 _k21 _k22: nat):
  $ _k1 = _k2 -> _op1 = _op2 -> _sz1 = _sz2 -> _ea1 = _ea2 -> _a1 = _a2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> (writeUnop _k1 _op1 _sz1 _ea1 _a1 _k21 <-> writeUnop _k2 _op2 _sz2 _ea2 _a2 _k22) $;

pub theorem writeUnopInc {w c o: nat} (k sz ea a k2: nat): $ writeUnop k (unopInc) sz ea a k2 <-> E. w E. c E. o (addCarry sz a 1 w c o /\ writeCFOFResult k sz ea w (CF (readFlags k)) (true o) k2) $;

pub theorem writeUnopDec {w c o: nat} (k sz ea a k2: nat): $ writeUnop k (unopDec) sz ea a k2 <-> E. w E. c E. o (subBorrow sz a 1 w c o /\ writeCFOFResult k sz ea w (CF (readFlags k)) (true o) k2) $;

pub theorem writeUnopNot (k sz ea a k2: nat): $ writeUnop k (unopNot) sz ea a k2 <-> writeEA k sz ea (bitsNot (wsizeBits sz) a) k2 $;

pub theorem writeUnopNeg {b: nat} (k sz ea a k2: nat): $ writeUnop k (unopNeg) sz ea a k2 <-> E. b (b = bitsNeg (wsizeBits sz) a /\ writeCFOFResult k sz ea b (a != 0) (MSB sz a /\ ~MSB sz b) k2) $;

pub theorem writeUnopT (k op sz ea a k2: nat): $ k e. Config /\ op e. ns (Unop) /\ sz e. WSize /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ ea e. EA /\ writeUnop k op sz ea a k2 -> k2 e. Config $;

def divModSz (sz a b d m: nat): wff;

theorem divModSzeqd (_G: wff) (_sz1 _sz2 _a1 _a2 _b1 _b2 _d1 _d2 _m1 _m2: nat):
  $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ >
  $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ >
  $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ >
  $ _G -> _d1 = _d2 $ >
  $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ >
  $ _G -> (divModSz _sz1 _a1 _b1 _d1 _m1 <-> divModSz _sz2 _a2 _b2 _d2 _m2) $;

theorem divModSzeq (_sz1 _sz2 _a1 _a2 _b1 _b2 _d1 _d2 _m1 _m2: nat): $ _sz1 = _sz2 -> _a1 = _a2 -> _b1 = _b2 -> _d1 = _d2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> (divModSz _sz1 _a1 _b1 _d1 _m1 <-> divModSz _sz2 _a2 _b2 _d2 _m2) $;

theorem divModSzeq1d (_G: wff) (_sz1 _sz2 a b d m: nat): $ _G -> _sz1 = _sz2 $ > $ _G -> (divModSz _sz1 a b d m <-> divModSz _sz2 a b d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq1 (_sz1 _sz2 a b d m: nat): $ _sz1 = _sz2 -> (divModSz _sz1 a b d m <-> divModSz _sz2 a b d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq2d (_G: wff) (sz _a1 _a2 b d m: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> (divModSz sz _a1 b d m <-> divModSz sz _a2 b d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq2 (sz _a1 _a2 b d m: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> (divModSz sz _a1 b d m <-> divModSz sz _a2 b d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq3d (_G: wff) (sz a _b1 _b2 d m: nat): $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ > $ _G -> (divModSz sz a _b1 d m <-> divModSz sz a _b2 d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq3 (sz a _b1 _b2 d m: nat): $ _b1 = _b2 -> (divModSz sz a _b1 d m <-> divModSz sz a _b2 d m) $;

theorem divModSzeq4d (_G: wff) (sz a b _d1 _d2 m: nat): $ _G -> _d1 = _d2 $ > $ _G -> (divModSz sz a b _d1 m <-> divModSz sz a b _d2 m) $;

theorem divModSzeq4 (sz a b _d1 _d2 m: nat): $ _d1 = _d2 -> (divModSz sz a b _d1 m <-> divModSz sz a b _d2 m) $;

theorem divModSzeq5d (_G: wff) (sz a b d _m1 _m2: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> (divModSz sz a b d _m1 <-> divModSz sz a b d _m2) $;

theorem divModSzeq5 (sz a b d _m1 _m2: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> (divModSz sz a b d _m1 <-> divModSz sz a b d _m2) $;

abstract def execXAST (k ast k2: nat): wff;

theorem execXASTeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _ast1 _ast2 _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _ast1 = _ast2 $ > $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (execXAST _k1 _ast1 _k21 <-> execXAST _k2 _ast2 _k22) $;

theorem execXASTeq (_k1 _k2 _ast1 _ast2 _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _ast1 = _ast2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> (execXAST _k1 _ast1 _k21 <-> execXAST _k2 _ast2 _k22) $;

theorem execXASTeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 ast k2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (execXAST _k1 ast k2 <-> execXAST _k2 ast k2) $;

theorem execXASTeq1 (_k1 _k2 ast k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (execXAST _k1 ast k2 <-> execXAST _k2 ast k2) $;

theorem execXASTeq2d (_G: wff) (k _ast1 _ast2 k2: nat): $ _G -> _ast1 = _ast2 $ > $ _G -> (execXAST k _ast1 k2 <-> execXAST k _ast2 k2) $;

theorem execXASTeq2 (k _ast1 _ast2 k2: nat): $ _ast1 = _ast2 -> (execXAST k _ast1 k2 <-> execXAST k _ast2 k2) $;

theorem execXASTeq3d (_G: wff) (k ast _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (execXAST k ast _k21 <-> execXAST k ast _k22) $;

theorem execXASTeq3 (k ast _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (execXAST k ast _k21 <-> execXAST k ast _k22) $;

pub theorem execXASTUnop {q: nat} (k op sz rm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastUnop op sz rm) k2 <-> E. q (readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) q /\ writeUnop k op sz (RM_EA k rm) q k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTBinop {d s: nat} (k op sz ds k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastBinop op sz ds) k2 <-> E. d E. s (readEA k sz (destEA k ds) d /\ readEA k sz (srcEA k ds) s /\ writeBinop k op sz (destEA k ds) d s k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTMul {n src res lo hi: nat} (k sz rm k2: nat):
  $ execXAST k (xastMul sz rm) k2 <->
    E. n E. src E. res (n = wsizeBits sz /\
      readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) src /\
      res = readRegSz k sz (RAX) * src /\
      ifp (n = 8) (k2 = writeReg k (wSz16) (RAX) res) (E. lo E. hi (splitBits ((n <> lo) : (n <> hi) : 0) res /\ k2 = writeReg (writeReg k sz (RAX) lo) sz (RDX) hi))) $;

pub theorem execXASTDiv {n a b d m: nat} (k sz rm k2: nat):
  $ execXAST k (xastDiv sz rm) k2 <->
    E. n E. a E. b E. d E. m (n = wsizeBits sz /\
      readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) b /\
      divModSz sz a b d m /\
      ifp
        (n = 8)
        (a = readRegSz k (wSz16) (RAX) /\ eraseFlags (writeReg k sz (RAX) (shl m 8 + d)) k2)
        (splitBits ((n <> readRegSz k sz (RAX)) : (n <> readRegSz k sz (RDX)) : 0) a /\ eraseFlags (writeReg (writeReg k sz (RAX) d) sz (RDX) m) k2)) $;

pub theorem execXASTLea (k sz ds k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastLea sz ds) k2 <-> writeEA k sz (destEA k ds) (EA_addr (srcEA k ds)) k2 $;

pub theorem execXASTMovZX {src: nat} (k sz ds sz2 k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastMovZX sz ds sz2) k2 <-> E. src (readEA k sz (srcEA k ds) src /\ writeEA k sz2 (destEA k ds) src k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTMovSX {src: nat} (k sz ds sz2 k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastMovSX sz ds sz2) k2 <-> E. src (readEA k sz (srcEA k ds) src /\ writeEA k sz2 (destEA k ds) (sExt (wsizeBits sz) (wsizeBits sz2) src) k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTXchg {v: nat} (k sz rm r k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastXchg sz rm r) k2 <-> E. v (readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) v /\ writeEA (writeReg k sz r v) sz (RM_EA k rm) (readRegSz k sz r) k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTCmpXchg {src acc dst ki: nat} (k sz rm r k2: nat):
  $ execXAST k (xastCmpXchg sz rm r) k2 <->
    E. src E. acc E. dst E. ki (acc = readRegSz k sz (RAX) /\
      readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) dst /\
      writeBinop k (binopCmp) sz (EA_r r) acc dst ki /\
      ifp (acc = dst) (writeEA ki sz (RM_EA k rm) (readRegSz k sz r) k2) (writeEA ki sz (EA_r (RAX)) dst k2)) $;

pub theorem execXASTXadd {v: nat} (k sz rm r k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastXadd sz rm r) k2 <-> E. v (readEA k sz (RM_EA k rm) v /\ writeBinop k (binopAdd) sz (RM_EA k rm) (readRegSz k sz r) v k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTCMov {v: nat} (k c sz ds k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastCMov c sz ds) k2 <-> ifp (readCond k c) (E. v (readEA k sz (srcEA k ds) v /\ writeEA k sz (destEA k ds) v k2)) (k2 = k) $;

pub theorem execXASTSetCC {v: nat} (k c b rm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastSetCC c b rm) k2 <-> writeEA k (wSz8 (true b)) (RM_EA k rm) (nat (readCond k c)) k2 $;

pub theorem execXASTJump {v: nat} (k rm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastJump rm) k2 <-> E. v (readEA k (wSz64) (RM_EA k rm) v /\ k2 = writeRIP k v) $;

pub theorem execXASTJCC (k c q k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastJCC c q) k2 <-> k2 = if (readCond k c) (writeRIP k (readRIP k +_64 q)) k $;

pub theorem execXASTCall {ki: nat} (k irm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastCall irm) k2 <-> E. ki (pushRIP k ki /\ EA_jump ki (immRM_EA k irm) k2) $;

pub theorem execXASTRet {ki: nat} (k q k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastRet q) k2 <-> E. ki (popRIP k ki /\ k2 = setReg ki (RSP) (readReg ki (RSP) +_64 q)) $;

pub theorem execXASTLeave (k k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastLeave) k2 <-> popWrite (setReg k (RSP) (readReg k (RBP))) (RM_reg (RBP)) k2 $;

pub theorem execXASTPush (k irm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastPush irm) k2 <-> pushImmRM k irm k2 $;

pub theorem execXASTPop (k rm k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastPop rm) k2 <-> popWrite k rm k2 $;

pub theorem execXASTCMC (k k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastCMC) k2 <-> k2 = writeFlags k (setCF (readFlags k) (~CF (readFlags k))) $;

pub theorem execXASTCLC (k k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastCLC) k2 <-> k2 = writeFlags k (setCF (readFlags k) F.) $;

pub theorem execXASTSTC (k k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastSTC) k2 <-> k2 = writeFlags k (setCF (readFlags k) T.) $;

pub theorem execXASTSysCall {r11: nat} (k k2: nat): $ execXAST k (xastSysCall) k2 <-> E. r11 (r11 e. ns (u64) /\ k2 = setException (setReg (setReg k (RCX) (readRIP k)) 11 r11) (suc (exSysCall))) $;

theorem splitSum (A B: set) (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G /\ a // 2 e. A -> a = b0 (a // 2) -> p $ > $ G /\ a // 2 e. B -> a = b1 (a // 2) -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. Sum A B -> p $;

theorem splitEq (A: set) (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff) {x: nat}: $ G /\ x e. A -> a = x -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. A -> p $;

theorem splitXp1 (A B: set) (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G /\ fst a e. A -> snd a e. B -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. Xp A B -> p $;

theorem splitXp2 (G: wff) (a b c: nat) (p: wff): $ G -> a = b <> c -> p $ > $ G -> snd a = c -> fst a = b -> p $;

theorem splitXpE (A B: set) (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff) {x: nat}: $ G /\ x e. A /\ snd a e. B -> fst a = x -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. Xp A B -> p $;

theorem splitOpt (A: set) (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G -> a = 0 -> p $ > $ G /\ a - 1 e. A -> a = suc (a - 1) -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. Option A -> p $;

theorem splitupto (G: wff) (a n: nat) (p: wff): $ G -> a = 0 -> p $ > $ G /\ a - 1 e. ns (upto n) -> a = suc (a - 1) -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. ns (upto (suc n)) -> p $;

theorem splitupto0 (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G /\ a e. ns (upto 0) -> p $;

theorem splitupto1 (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G -> a = 0 -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. ns (upto 1) -> p $;

theorem splitBool (G: wff) (a: nat) (p: wff): $ G -> a = 0 -> p $ > $ G -> a = 1 -> p $ > $ G /\ a e. ns (Bool) -> p $;

pub theorem execXAST_T (k ast k2: nat): $ k e. Config /\ ast e. XAST /\ execXAST k ast k2 -> k2 e. Config $;

def step (k k2: nat): wff;

theorem stepeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (step _k1 _k21 <-> step _k2 _k22) $;

theorem stepeq (_k1 _k2 _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> (step _k1 _k21 <-> step _k2 _k22) $;

theorem stepeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 k2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (step _k1 k2 <-> step _k2 k2) $;

theorem stepeq1 (_k1 _k2 k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (step _k1 k2 <-> step _k2 k2) $;

theorem stepeq2d (_G: wff) (k _k21 _k22: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (step k _k21 <-> step k _k22) $;

theorem stepeq2 (k _k21 _k22: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (step k _k21 <-> step k _k22) $;

pub theorem stepT (k k2: nat): $ step k k2 -> k e. Config /\ k2 e. Config $;

def PageMapping (M: nat): set;

theorem PageMappingeqd (_G: wff) (_M1 _M2: nat): $ _G -> _M1 = _M2 $ > $ _G -> PageMapping _M1 == PageMapping _M2 $;

theorem PageMappingeq (_M1 _M2: nat): $ _M1 = _M2 -> PageMapping _M1 == PageMapping _M2 $;

theorem elPageMapping (M: nat) {a: nat} (m: nat) {p v: nat}: $ m e. PageMapping M <-> m e. Arrow (ns (u64)) (Option (Prot)) /\ A. a A. p (a <> suc p e. ns m -> E. v ns M @ a = p <> v) $;

theorem PageMappingss (M: nat): $ PageMapping M C_ Arrow (ns (u64)) (Option (Prot)) $;

theorem finPageMapping (M: nat): $ finite (PageMapping M) $;

theorem writePM (G: wff) (a m m2 prot x y: nat): $ G -> ns m @ a = prot <> x $ > $ G -> ns m2 == write (ns m) a (prot <> y) $ > $ G -> PageMapping m C_ PageMapping m2 $;

theorem writeMemory1PM (a b e m m2: nat): $ writeMemory1 m a b m2 e -> PageMapping m C_ PageMapping m2 $;

theorem writeMemoryPM (a e l m m2: nat): $ writeMemory m a l m2 e -> PageMapping m C_ PageMapping m2 $;

theorem writeMemPM (a k k2 l: nat): $ writeMem k a l k2 -> PageMapping (getMemory k) C_ PageMapping (getMemory k2) $;

def KernelState: set;

def mkKS (i o k m: nat): nat;

theorem mkKSeqd (_G: wff) (_i1 _i2 _o1 _o2 _k1 _k2 _m1 _m2: nat): $ _G -> _i1 = _i2 $ > $ _G -> _o1 = _o2 $ > $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> mkKS _i1 _o1 _k1 _m1 = mkKS _i2 _o2 _k2 _m2 $;

theorem mkKSeq (_i1 _i2 _o1 _o2 _k1 _k2 _m1 _m2: nat): $ _i1 = _i2 -> _o1 = _o2 -> _k1 = _k2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> mkKS _i1 _o1 _k1 _m1 = mkKS _i2 _o2 _k2 _m2 $;

theorem mkKSeq1d (_G: wff) (_i1 _i2 o k m: nat): $ _G -> _i1 = _i2 $ > $ _G -> mkKS _i1 o k m = mkKS _i2 o k m $;

theorem mkKSeq1 (_i1 _i2 o k m: nat): $ _i1 = _i2 -> mkKS _i1 o k m = mkKS _i2 o k m $;

theorem mkKSeq2d (_G: wff) (i _o1 _o2 k m: nat): $ _G -> _o1 = _o2 $ > $ _G -> mkKS i _o1 k m = mkKS i _o2 k m $;

theorem mkKSeq2 (i _o1 _o2 k m: nat): $ _o1 = _o2 -> mkKS i _o1 k m = mkKS i _o2 k m $;

theorem mkKSeq3d (_G: wff) (i o _k1 _k2 m: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> mkKS i o _k1 m = mkKS i o _k2 m $;

theorem mkKSeq3 (i o _k1 _k2 m: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> mkKS i o _k1 m = mkKS i o _k2 m $;

theorem mkKSeq4d (_G: wff) (i o k _m1 _m2: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> mkKS i o k _m1 = mkKS i o k _m2 $;

theorem mkKSeq4 (i o k _m1 _m2: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> mkKS i o k _m1 = mkKS i o k _m2 $;

pub theorem mkKS_T (i o k m: nat): $ mkKS i o k m e. KernelState <-> i e. List (ns (u8)) /\ o e. List (ns (u8)) /\ k e. Config /\ m e. PageMapping (getMemory k) $;

theorem mkKS_ex {i k: nat} (ks: nat) {m o: nat}: $ E. i E. o E. k E. m ks = mkKS i o k m $;

local def setMapping (ks k2 m2: nat): nat;

theorem setMappingeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _k21 _k22 _m21 _m22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> _m21 = _m22 $ > $ _G -> setMapping _ks1 _k21 _m21 = setMapping _ks2 _k22 _m22 $;

theorem setMappingeq (_ks1 _ks2 _k21 _k22 _m21 _m22: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> _m21 = _m22 -> setMapping _ks1 _k21 _m21 = setMapping _ks2 _k22 _m22 $;

theorem setMappingeq1d (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 k2 m2: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> setMapping _ks1 k2 m2 = setMapping _ks2 k2 m2 $;

theorem setMappingeq1 (_ks1 _ks2 k2 m2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> setMapping _ks1 k2 m2 = setMapping _ks2 k2 m2 $;

theorem setMappingeq2d (_G: wff) (ks _k21 _k22 m2: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> setMapping ks _k21 m2 = setMapping ks _k22 m2 $;

def writeMapping (ks k2 m2 ks2: nat): wff;

theorem writeMappingeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _k21 _k22 _m21 _m22 _ks21 _ks22: nat):
  $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ >
  $ _G -> _m21 = _m22 $ >
  $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ >
  $ _G -> (writeMapping _ks1 _k21 _m21 _ks21 <-> writeMapping _ks2 _k22 _m22 _ks22) $;

theorem writeMappingeq1 (_ks1 _ks2 k2 m2 ks2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> (writeMapping _ks1 k2 m2 ks2 <-> writeMapping _ks2 k2 m2 ks2) $;

theorem writeMappingeq2d (_G: wff) (ks _k21 _k22 m2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (writeMapping ks _k21 m2 ks2 <-> writeMapping ks _k22 m2 ks2) $;

theorem writeMappingeq2 (ks _k21 _k22 m2 ks2: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (writeMapping ks _k21 m2 ks2 <-> writeMapping ks _k22 m2 ks2) $;

theorem writeMappingeq3d (_G: wff) (ks k2 _m21 _m22 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _m21 = _m22 $ > $ _G -> (writeMapping ks k2 _m21 ks2 <-> writeMapping ks k2 _m22 ks2) $;

theorem writeMappingeq3 (ks k2 _m21 _m22 ks2: nat): $ _m21 = _m22 -> (writeMapping ks k2 _m21 ks2 <-> writeMapping ks k2 _m22 ks2) $;

theorem writeMappingeq4d (_G: wff) (ks k2 m2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (writeMapping ks k2 m2 _ks21 <-> writeMapping ks k2 m2 _ks22) $;

theorem writeMappingeq4 (ks k2 m2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (writeMapping ks k2 m2 _ks21 <-> writeMapping ks k2 m2 _ks22) $;

pub theorem writeMappingT (ks m k ks2: nat): $ writeMapping ks k m ks2 -> ks e. KernelState /\ k e. Config /\ m e. PageMapping (getMemory k) /\ ks2 e. KernelState $;

local def setCfg (ks k2: nat): nat;

def writeCfg (ks k2 ks2: nat): wff;

theorem writeCfgeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _k21 _k22 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (writeCfg _ks1 _k21 _ks21 <-> writeCfg _ks2 _k22 _ks22) $;

  $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ >
  $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ >
  $ _G -> _b1 = _b2 $ >

abstract def mapMemory (prot m a l: nat): nat;

theorem mapMemoryeq1d (_G: wff) (_prot1 _prot2 m a l: nat): $ _G -> _prot1 = _prot2 $ > $ _G -> mapMemory _prot1 m a l = mapMemory _prot2 m a l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq1 (_prot1 _prot2 m a l: nat): $ _prot1 = _prot2 -> mapMemory _prot1 m a l = mapMemory _prot2 m a l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq2d (_G: wff) (prot _m1 _m2 a l: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> mapMemory prot _m1 a l = mapMemory prot _m2 a l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq2 (prot _m1 _m2 a l: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> mapMemory prot _m1 a l = mapMemory prot _m2 a l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq3d (_G: wff) (prot m _a1 _a2 l: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> mapMemory prot m _a1 l = mapMemory prot m _a2 l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq3 (prot m _a1 _a2 l: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> mapMemory prot m _a1 l = mapMemory prot m _a2 l $;

theorem mapMemoryeq4d (_G: wff) (prot m a _l1 _l2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> mapMemory prot m a _l1 = mapMemory prot m a _l2 $;

theorem mapMemoryeq4 (prot m a _l1 _l2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> mapMemory prot m a _l1 = mapMemory prot m a _l2 $;

pub theorem mapMemory0 {x: nat} (prot m a: nat): $ prot e. Prot /\ m e. X\ x e. Memory, PageMapping x /\ a e. ns (u64) -> mapMemory prot m a 0 = m $;

pub theorem mapMemoryS {x: nat} (prot m a b l: nat):
  $ prot e. Prot /\ m e. X\ x e. Memory, PageMapping x /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ b e. ns (u8) /\ l e. List (ns (u8)) -> mapMemory prot m a (b : l) = mapMemory prot (mapMemory1 prot m a b) (a +_64 1) l $;

pub theorem mapMemoryT {x: nat} (prot m a l: nat): $ prot e. Prot /\ m e. X\ x e. Memory, PageMapping x /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ l e. List (ns (u8)) -> mapMemory prot m a l e. X\ x e. Memory, PageMapping x $;

def mapMem (prot k km a l k2 km2: nat): wff;

theorem mapMemeqd (_G: wff) (_prot1 _prot2 _k1 _k2 _km1 _km2 _a1 _a2 _l1 _l2 _k21 _k22 _km21 _km22: nat):
  $ _G -> _prot1 = _prot2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _km1 = _km2 $ >
  $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ >
  $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ >
  $ _G -> _km21 = _km22 $ >
  $ _G -> (mapMem _prot1 _k1 _km1 _a1 _l1 _k21 _km21 <-> mapMem _prot2 _k2 _km2 _a2 _l2 _k22 _km22) $;

theorem mapMemeq (_prot1 _prot2 _k1 _k2 _km1 _km2 _a1 _a2 _l1 _l2 _k21 _k22 _km21 _km22: nat):
  $ _prot1 = _prot2 ->
    _k1 = _k2 ->
    _km1 = _km2 ->
    _a1 = _a2 ->
    _l1 = _l2 ->
    _k21 = _k22 ->
    _km21 = _km22 ->
    (mapMem _prot1 _k1 _km1 _a1 _l1 _k21 _km21 <-> mapMem _prot2 _k2 _km2 _a2 _l2 _k22 _km22) $;

theorem mapMemeq1d (_G: wff) (_prot1 _prot2 k km a l k2 km2: nat): $ _G -> _prot1 = _prot2 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem _prot1 k km a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem _prot2 k km a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq1 (_prot1 _prot2 k km a l k2 km2: nat): $ _prot1 = _prot2 -> (mapMem _prot1 k km a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem _prot2 k km a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq2d (_G: wff) (prot _k1 _k2 km a l k2 km2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot _k1 km a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot _k2 km a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq2 (prot _k1 _k2 km a l k2 km2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (mapMem prot _k1 km a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot _k2 km a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq3d (_G: wff) (prot k _km1 _km2 a l k2 km2: nat): $ _G -> _km1 = _km2 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot k _km1 a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k _km2 a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq3 (prot k _km1 _km2 a l k2 km2: nat): $ _km1 = _km2 -> (mapMem prot k _km1 a l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k _km2 a l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq4d (_G: wff) (prot k km _a1 _a2 l k2 km2: nat): $ _G -> _a1 = _a2 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot k km _a1 l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km _a2 l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq4 (prot k km _a1 _a2 l k2 km2: nat): $ _a1 = _a2 -> (mapMem prot k km _a1 l k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km _a2 l k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq5d (_G: wff) (prot k km a _l1 _l2 k2 km2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot k km a _l1 k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km a _l2 k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq5 (prot k km a _l1 _l2 k2 km2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> (mapMem prot k km a _l1 k2 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km a _l2 k2 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq6d (_G: wff) (prot k km a l _k21 _k22 km2: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot k km a l _k21 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km a l _k22 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq6 (prot k km a l _k21 _k22 km2: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (mapMem prot k km a l _k21 km2 <-> mapMem prot k km a l _k22 km2) $;

theorem mapMemeq7d (_G: wff) (prot k km a l k2 _km21 _km22: nat): $ _G -> _km21 = _km22 $ > $ _G -> (mapMem prot k km a l k2 _km21 <-> mapMem prot k km a l k2 _km22) $;

theorem mapMemeq7 (prot k km a l k2 _km21 _km22: nat): $ _km21 = _km22 -> (mapMem prot k km a l k2 _km21 <-> mapMem prot k km a l k2 _km22) $;

pub theorem mapMemT (prot k km a l k2 km2: nat):
  $ mapMem prot k km a l k2 km2 -> prot e. Prot /\ k e. Config /\ km e. PageMapping (getMemory k) /\ a e. ns (u64) /\ l e. List (ns (u8)) /\ k2 e. Config /\ km2 e. PageMapping (getMemory k2) $;

def sys_mmap: nat;

def MAP_PRIVATE: nat;

def MAP_ANONYMOUS: nat;

def execMMap (k m k2 m2 ret: nat): wff;

theorem execMMapeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _k21 _k22 _m21 _m22 _ret1 _ret2: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ >
  $ _G -> _m21 = _m22 $ >
  $ _G -> _ret1 = _ret2 $ >
  $ _G -> (execMMap _k1 _m1 _k21 _m21 _ret1 <-> execMMap _k2 _m2 _k22 _m22 _ret2) $;

theorem execMMapeq (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _k21 _k22 _m21 _m22 _ret1 _ret2: nat):
  $ _k1 = _k2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> _k21 = _k22 -> _m21 = _m22 -> _ret1 = _ret2 -> (execMMap _k1 _m1 _k21 _m21 _ret1 <-> execMMap _k2 _m2 _k22 _m22 _ret2) $;

theorem execMMapeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 m k2 m2 ret: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (execMMap _k1 m k2 m2 ret <-> execMMap _k2 m k2 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq1 (_k1 _k2 m k2 m2 ret: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (execMMap _k1 m k2 m2 ret <-> execMMap _k2 m k2 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq2d (_G: wff) (k _m1 _m2 k2 m2 ret: nat): $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ > $ _G -> (execMMap k _m1 k2 m2 ret <-> execMMap k _m2 k2 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq2 (k _m1 _m2 k2 m2 ret: nat): $ _m1 = _m2 -> (execMMap k _m1 k2 m2 ret <-> execMMap k _m2 k2 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq3d (_G: wff) (k m _k21 _k22 m2 ret: nat): $ _G -> _k21 = _k22 $ > $ _G -> (execMMap k m _k21 m2 ret <-> execMMap k m _k22 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq3 (k m _k21 _k22 m2 ret: nat): $ _k21 = _k22 -> (execMMap k m _k21 m2 ret <-> execMMap k m _k22 m2 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq4d (_G: wff) (k m k2 _m21 _m22 ret: nat): $ _G -> _m21 = _m22 $ > $ _G -> (execMMap k m k2 _m21 ret <-> execMMap k m k2 _m22 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq4 (k m k2 _m21 _m22 ret: nat): $ _m21 = _m22 -> (execMMap k m k2 _m21 ret <-> execMMap k m k2 _m22 ret) $;

theorem execMMapeq5d (_G: wff) (k m k2 m2 _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _G -> _ret1 = _ret2 $ > $ _G -> (execMMap k m k2 m2 _ret1 <-> execMMap k m k2 m2 _ret2) $;

theorem execMMapeq5 (k m k2 m2 _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _ret1 = _ret2 -> (execMMap k m k2 m2 _ret1 <-> execMMap k m k2 m2 _ret2) $;

pub theorem execMMapT (k m k2 m2 ret: nat): $ execMMap k m k2 m2 ret -> k e. Config /\ m e. PageMapping (getMemory k) /\ k2 e. Config /\ m2 e. PageMapping (getMemory k2) /\ ret e. ns (u64) $;

def execIO (ks ks2: nat): wff;

theorem execIOeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (execIO _ks1 _ks21 <-> execIO _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem execIOeq (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> _ks21 = _ks22 -> (execIO _ks1 _ks21 <-> execIO _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem execIOeq1d (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> (execIO _ks1 ks2 <-> execIO _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem execIOeq1 (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> (execIO _ks1 ks2 <-> execIO _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem execIOeq2d (_G: wff) (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (execIO ks _ks21 <-> execIO ks _ks22) $;

theorem execIOeq2 (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (execIO ks _ks21 <-> execIO ks _ks22) $;

pub theorem execIO_T (ks ks2: nat): $ ks e. KernelState /\ execIO ks ks2 -> ks2 e. KernelState $;

def sys_exit: nat;

def execExit (k ret: nat): wff;

theorem execExiteqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _ret1 = _ret2 $ > $ _G -> (execExit _k1 _ret1 <-> execExit _k2 _ret2) $;

theorem execExiteq (_k1 _k2 _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _ret1 = _ret2 -> (execExit _k1 _ret1 <-> execExit _k2 _ret2) $;

theorem execExiteq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 ret: nat): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (execExit _k1 ret <-> execExit _k2 ret) $;

theorem execExiteq1 (_k1 _k2 ret: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (execExit _k1 ret <-> execExit _k2 ret) $;

theorem execExiteq2d (_G: wff) (k _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _G -> _ret1 = _ret2 $ > $ _G -> (execExit k _ret1 <-> execExit k _ret2) $;

theorem execExiteq2 (k _ret1 _ret2: nat): $ _ret1 = _ret2 -> (execExit k _ret1 <-> execExit k _ret2) $;

pub theorem execExitT (k ret: nat): $ execExit k ret -> k e. Config /\ ret e. ns (u32) $;

theorem execExit_determ (k ret: nat): $ execExit k ret /\ execExit k 0 -> ret = 0 $;

def ksStep (ks ks2: nat): wff;

theorem ksStepeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksStep _ks1 _ks21 <-> ksStep _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksStepeq (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksStep _ks1 _ks21 <-> ksStep _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksStepeq1d (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> (ksStep _ks1 ks2 <-> ksStep _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem ksStepeq1 (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> (ksStep _ks1 ks2 <-> ksStep _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem ksStepeq2d (_G: wff) (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksStep ks _ks21 <-> ksStep ks _ks22) $;

theorem ksStepeq2 (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksStep ks _ks21 <-> ksStep ks _ks22) $;

pub theorem ksStepT (ks ks2: nat): $ ksStep ks ks2 -> ks e. KernelState /\ ks2 e. KernelState $;

theorem ksStep_no_exit (ks ks2 ret: nat): $ ksStep ks ks2 -> ~execExit (ksCfg ks) ret $;

local def ksPath_aux (ksl ks2: nat): wff;

theorem ksPath_auxeqd (_G: wff) (_ksl1 _ksl2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ksl1 = _ksl2 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath_aux _ksl1 _ks21 <-> ksPath_aux _ksl2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksPath_auxeq (_ksl1 _ksl2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ksl1 = _ksl2 -> _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksPath_aux _ksl1 _ks21 <-> ksPath_aux _ksl2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksPath_auxeq1d (_G: wff) (_ksl1 _ksl2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _ksl1 = _ksl2 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath_aux _ksl1 ks2 <-> ksPath_aux _ksl2 ks2) $;

theorem ksPath_auxeq1 (_ksl1 _ksl2 ks2: nat): $ _ksl1 = _ksl2 -> (ksPath_aux _ksl1 ks2 <-> ksPath_aux _ksl2 ks2) $;

theorem ksPath_auxeq2d (_G: wff) (ksl _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath_aux ksl _ks21 <-> ksPath_aux ksl _ks22) $;

theorem ksPath_auxeq2 (ksl _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksPath_aux ksl _ks21 <-> ksPath_aux ksl _ks22) $;

theorem ksPath_aux_val {i ks: nat} (ks1 ks2 l: nat) {l2: nat}: $ ksPath_aux (ks1 <> l) ks2 <-> l e. ocasep (ks2 = ks1) (S\ ks, {l2 | ksStep ks1 ks /\ ks <> l2 e. ns (sep (upto (ks1 <> l)) {i | ksPath_aux i ks2})}) $;

local def ksPath (ks l ks2: nat): wff;

theorem ksPatheqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _l1 _l2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath _ks1 _l1 _ks21 <-> ksPath _ks2 _l2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksPatheq (_ks1 _ks2 _l1 _l2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> _l1 = _l2 -> _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksPath _ks1 _l1 _ks21 <-> ksPath _ks2 _l2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksPatheq1d (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 l ks2: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath _ks1 l ks2 <-> ksPath _ks2 l ks2) $;

theorem ksPatheq1 (_ks1 _ks2 l ks2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> (ksPath _ks1 l ks2 <-> ksPath _ks2 l ks2) $;

theorem ksPatheq2d (_G: wff) (ks _l1 _l2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _l1 = _l2 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath ks _l1 ks2 <-> ksPath ks _l2 ks2) $;

theorem ksPatheq2 (ks _l1 _l2 ks2: nat): $ _l1 = _l2 -> (ksPath ks _l1 ks2 <-> ksPath ks _l2 ks2) $;

theorem ksPatheq3d (_G: wff) (ks l _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksPath ks l _ks21 <-> ksPath ks l _ks22) $;

theorem ksPatheq3 (ks l _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksPath ks l _ks21 <-> ksPath ks l _ks22) $;

theorem ksPath0 (ks ks2: nat): $ ksPath ks 0 ks2 <-> ks e. KernelState /\ ks2 = ks $;

theorem ksPathS (ks ks2 l ks3: nat): $ ksPath ks (ks2 : l) ks3 <-> ksStep ks ks2 /\ ksPath ks2 l ks3 $;

theorem ksPathT (ks l ks2: nat): $ ksPath ks l ks2 -> ks e. KernelState /\ all (KernelState) l /\ ks2 e. KernelState $;

abstract def ksReachable (ks ks2: nat): wff;

theorem ksReachableeqd (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksReachable _ks1 _ks21 <-> ksReachable _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksReachableeq (_ks1 _ks2 _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksReachable _ks1 _ks21 <-> ksReachable _ks2 _ks22) $;

theorem ksReachableeq1d (_G: wff) (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> (ksReachable _ks1 ks2 <-> ksReachable _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem ksReachableeq1 (_ks1 _ks2 ks2: nat): $ _ks1 = _ks2 -> (ksReachable _ks1 ks2 <-> ksReachable _ks2 ks2) $;

theorem ksReachableeq2d (_G: wff) (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _G -> _ks21 = _ks22 $ > $ _G -> (ksReachable ks _ks21 <-> ksReachable ks _ks22) $;

theorem ksReachableeq2 (ks _ks21 _ks22: nat): $ _ks21 = _ks22 -> (ksReachable ks _ks21 <-> ksReachable ks _ks22) $;

pub theorem ksReachable0 (ks: nat): $ ks e. KernelState -> ksReachable ks ks $;

pub theorem ksReachableS (ks ks2 ks3: nat): $ ksStep ks ks2 -> ksReachable ks2 ks3 -> ksReachable ks ks3 $;

pub theorem ksReachableInd {ks1 ks2: nat} (ks ks3: nat) (A: set): $ ks e. A /\ A. ks1 A. ks2 (ksStep ks1 ks2 -> ks1 e. A -> ks2 e. A) /\ ksReachable ks ks3 -> ks3 e. A $;

theorem ksReachable_ind (G: wff) (ks: nat) {ks1 ks2: nat} (ks3: nat) (p0 p3: wff) {x: nat} (p: wff x) (p1: wff ks1) (p2: wff ks2):
  $ G -> ksReachable ks ks3 $ >
  $ x = ks3 -> (p <-> p3) $ >
  $ x = ks -> (p <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = ks1 -> (p <-> p1) $ >
  $ x = ks2 -> (p <-> p2) $ >
  $ G -> p0 $ >
  $ G /\ ksStep ks1 ks2 /\ p1 -> p2 $ >
  $ G -> p3 $;

theorem ksReachableInd_rev (A: set) (ks: nat) {ks1 ks2: nat} (ksr: nat): $ ksr e. A /\ A. ks1 A. ks2 (ksStep ks1 ks2 -> ks2 e. A -> ks1 e. A) /\ ksReachable ks ksr -> ks e. A $;

theorem ksReachable_rind (G: wff) (ks: nat) {ks1 ks2: nat} (ks3: nat) (p0 p3: wff) {x: nat} (p: wff x) (p1: wff ks1) (p2: wff ks2):
  $ G -> ksReachable ks ks3 $ >
  $ x = ks -> (p <-> p0) $ >
  $ x = ks1 -> (p <-> p1) $ >
  $ x = ks2 -> (p <-> p2) $ >
  $ x = ks3 -> (p <-> p3) $ >
  $ G -> p3 $ >
  $ G /\ ksStep ks1 ks2 /\ p2 -> p1 $ >
  $ G -> p0 $;

pub theorem ksReachableT (ks ks2: nat): $ ksReachable ks ks2 -> ks e. KernelState /\ ks2 e. KernelState $;

theorem ksReachable_hd (ks: nat) {ks2: nat} (ks3: nat): $ ksReachable ks ks3 <-> ks e. KernelState /\ ks = ks3 \/ E. ks2 (ksStep ks ks2 /\ ksReachable ks2 ks3) $;

theorem ksReachable1 (ks ks2: nat): $ ksStep ks ks2 -> ksReachable ks ks2 $;

theorem ksReachable_tr (ks ks2 ks3: nat): $ ksReachable ks ks2 -> ksReachable ks2 ks3 -> ksReachable ks ks3 $;

theorem ksReachable_exit (ks ks2 ret: nat): $ execExit (ksCfg ks) ret -> ksReachable ks ks2 -> ks2 = ks $;

def terminates_ensuring (k: nat) (P: set): wff;

theorem terminates_ensuringeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _P1 == _P2 $ > $ _G -> (terminates_ensuring _k1 _P1 <-> terminates_ensuring _k2 _P2) $;

theorem terminates_ensuringeq (_k1 _k2: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _P1 == _P2 -> (terminates_ensuring _k1 _P1 <-> terminates_ensuring _k2 _P2) $;

theorem terminates_ensuringeq1d (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat) (P: set): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> (terminates_ensuring _k1 P <-> terminates_ensuring _k2 P) $;

theorem terminates_ensuringeq1 (_k1 _k2: nat) (P: set): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (terminates_ensuring _k1 P <-> terminates_ensuring _k2 P) $;

theorem terminates_ensuringeq2d (_G: wff) (k: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _G -> _P1 == _P2 $ > $ _G -> (terminates_ensuring k _P1 <-> terminates_ensuring k _P2) $;

theorem terminates_ensuringeq2 (k: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _P1 == _P2 -> (terminates_ensuring k _P1 <-> terminates_ensuring k _P2) $;

pub theorem terminates_ensuringT (k: nat) (P: set): $ terminates_ensuring k P -> k e. KernelState $;

local def can_terminate_ensuring (k: nat) (P: set): wff;

theorem can_terminate_ensuringeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ > $ _G -> _P1 == _P2 $ > $ _G -> (can_terminate_ensuring _k1 _P1 <-> can_terminate_ensuring _k2 _P2) $;

theorem can_terminate_ensuringeq (_k1 _k2: nat) (_P1 _P2: set): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _P1 == _P2 -> (can_terminate_ensuring _k1 _P1 <-> can_terminate_ensuring _k2 _P2) $;

theorem blankConfigeq1 (_entry1 _entry2 k: nat): $ _entry1 = _entry2 -> (blankConfig _entry1 k <-> blankConfig _entry2 k) $;

theorem blankConfigeq2 (entry _k1 _k2: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> (blankConfig entry _k1 <-> blankConfig entry _k2) $;

def allocStack (k m k3 km3: nat): wff;

theorem allocStackeqd (_G: wff) (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _k31 _k32 _km31 _km32: nat):
  $ _G -> _k1 = _k2 $ >
  $ _G -> _m1 = _m2 $ >
  $ _G -> _k31 = _k32 $ >
  $ _G -> _km31 = _km32 $ >
  $ _G -> (allocStack _k1 _m1 _k31 _km31 <-> allocStack _k2 _m2 _k32 _km32) $;

theorem allocStackeq (_k1 _k2 _m1 _m2 _k31 _k32 _km31 _km32: nat): $ _k1 = _k2 -> _m1 = _m2 -> _k31 = _k32 -> _km31 = _km32 -> (allocStack _k1 _m1 _k31 _km31 <-> allocStack _k2 _m2 _k32 _km32) $;

def initialConfig (elf: string) (i ks: nat): wff;

local def initialConfig2 (elf i ks: nat): wff;

theorem initialConfig2eqd (_G: wff) (_elf1 _elf2 _i1 _i2 _ks1 _ks2: nat): $ _G -> _elf1 = _elf2 $ > $ _G -> _i1 = _i2 $ > $ _G -> _ks1 = _ks2 $ > $ _G -> (initialConfig2 _elf1 _i1 _ks1 <-> initialConfig2 _elf2 _i2 _ks2) $;

theorem initialConfig2eq2 (elf _i1 _i2 ks: nat): $ _i1 = _i2 -> (initialConfig2 elf _i1 ks <-> initialConfig2 elf _i2 ks) $;
